[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m## Findings[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m1. **No version drift possible.** With path-only deps and no SemVer pinning, "current version" = "source-declared version" = 0.1.0 for all 6. Updating a source `Cargo.toml` propagates instantly. There is no registry-side lag to chase.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m2. **No crates.io publication.** 3 crates have `publish = true` (or default `true`): `pheno-otel`, `pheno-port-adapter`, `pheno-errors`. None are actually published. 3 are explicitly `publish = false`: `pheno-context`, `pheno-config`, `pheno-cli-base`. The crates.io audit dimension is empty by design.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m3. **No "outdated dep" condition exists.** The audit's stated goal (list crates where current < latest) returns 0 actionable items, because there is no `latest` to compare against. This is consistent with the project's monorepo substrate design (ADR-013 / ADR-022 / ADR-023): reusable capabilities are vendored as sibling crates, not consumed from a registry.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m4. **Reproducibility gap (out of scope but worth noting).** Path-only deps break air-gapped builds and create submodule-drift risk. If reproducibility matters, switch to `git = "https://github.com/KooshaPari/<repo>", tag = "v0.1.0"` for the 3 publishable crates. This is a separate hardening track, not an "outdated dep" issue.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m5. **Mirror-source drift (also out of scope).** `pheno-otel`, `pheno-port-adapter`, `pheno-errors`, `pheno-context` each exist at multiple paths. Mirrors declare identical versions (0.1.0) and identical core metadata, but a deeper diff (e.g. `[dependencies]` divergence, README drift) was not part of this audit. Recommend a follow-up mirror-vs-canonical diff if drift becomes a concern.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m6. **Substrate canonicalization status:**[m
[32m+[m[32m   - `pheno-otel` ✓ canonical per ADR-037; consumed by 15 crates correctly.[m
[32m+[m[32m   - `pheno-port-adapter` ✓ canonical per ADR-038; consumed as sibling source in workspaces.[m
[32m+[m[32m   - `pheno-errors` ✓ canonical (AppError substrate); consumed by 3 crates correctly.[m
[32m+[m[32m   - `pheno-context` ✓ FocalPoint workspace member; not published.[m
[32m+[m[32m   - `pheno-config` ✓ canonical per ADR-022 (Rust core); Configra is canonical repo per ADR-031; consumed by 2 crates.[m
[32m+[m[32m   - `pheno-cli-base` ✓ FocalPoint workspace member; consumed by 3 crates.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m## Recommendation[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mTreat the absence of a crates.io delta as a confirmation that the monorepo's path-dep design is working as intended for an internal fleet. No `cargo update` / `cargo bump` action is required. If the team wants a "published substrate" track for downstream external consumers, that's a separate plan (publish `pheno-otel`, `pheno-port-adapter`, `pheno-errors` to crates.io with semver + CHANGELOG hygiene per ADR-040).[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m

[32m+[m[32m## The 5 tests added[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### 1. `tests::log_warn_actually_emits_tracing_event`[m
[32m+[m[32m**File:** `pheno-errors/src/lib.rs:347-379`[m
[32m+[m[32m**Closes:** `AppError::log_warn` (`lib.rs:172-179`)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mThe existing `log_warn_preserves_error` (`lib.rs:331-335`) only checked that[m
[32m+[m[32mthe function returned the same value (passthrough). It never asserted the[m
[32m+[m[32memit side-effect — i.e., that `tracing::warn!` actually fires with the[m
[32m+[m[32mstructured fields. Without this test, `log_warn` could be silently[m
[32m+[m[32mrefactored to a no-op and the suite would still be green.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mUses `#[traced_test]` from `tracing-test = "0.2"` to capture events.[m
[32m+[m[32mAsserts four things:[m
[32m+[m[32m1. Return value preserved (passthrough contract).[m
[32m+[m[32m2. `logs_contain("error")`, `logs_contain("validation")`,[m
[32m+[m[32m   `logs_contain("email format invalid")` — message field + kind tag +[m
[32m+[m[32m   display string all surfaced.[m
[32m+[m[32m3. `logs_contain("WARN")` — correct level.[m
[32m+[m[32m4. `!logs_contain("ERROR")` — must NOT promote to ERROR.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### 2. `tests::log_error_actually_emits_tracing_event`[m
[32m+[m[32m**File:** `pheno-errors/src/lib.rs:381-412`[m
[32m+[m[32m**Closes:** `AppError::log_error` (`lib.rs:185-192`)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mSame gap as test 1, but for the ERROR-level helper. Asserts:[m
[32m+[m[32m1. Return value preserved.[m
[32m+[m[32m2. `logs_contain("storage")`, `logs_contain("disk write failed")` —[m
[32m+[m[32m   structured fields surface.[m
[32m+[m[32m3. `logs_contain("ERROR")` — level must be ERROR (distinct from[m
[32m+[m[32m   `log_warn`'s WARN).[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mThese two tests together pin the **level-promotion semantics** that[m
[32m+[m[32mdistinguish the two helpers, which was previously only documented in[m
[32m+[m[32mdoc-comments and never asserted.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### 3. `rfc7807::tests::not_found_sets_instance_field`[m
[32m+[m[32m**File:** `pheno-errors/src/rfc7807.rs:269-293`[m
[32m+[m[32m**Closes:** `From<&AppError>` NotFound branch — `with_instance(format!("{entity}/{id}"))` at `rfc7807.rs:154`[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mThe existing `not_found_maps_to_404` (`rfc7807.rs:174-189`) checks[m
[32m+[m[32mstatus, title, detail, and problem_type. It **never reads[m
[32m+[m[32m`problem.instance`**, so the `with_instance(...)` call at line 154 was[m
[32m+[m[32msilently untested. A future refactor could drop that line and the suite[m
[32m+[m[32mwould still pass.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mAsserts:[m
[32m+[m[32m1. `problem.instance == Some("order/ord_abc123")` — follows the[m
[32m+[m[32m   `{entity}/{id}` convention.[m
[32m+[m[32m2. `json.contains("\"instance\":\"order/ord_abc123\"")` — round-trips[m
[32m+[m[32m   through the wire format.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### 4. `rfc7807::tests::problem_new_constructor_isolated_fields`[m
[32m+[m[32m**File:** `pheno-errors/src/rfc7807.rs:295-327`[m
[32m+[m[32m**Closes:** `Problem::new` constructor (`rfc7807.rs:92-100`)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m`Problem::new` was only ever tested **chained** with `with_type(...)` /[m
[32m+[m[32m`with_instance(...)` (see `builder_round_trips` at `rfc7807.rs:237-245`).[m
[32m+[m[32mThe constructor's own behavior — "set the three required-ish fields,[m
[32m+[m[32mleave problem_type and instance as `None`" — was inferred but never[m
[32m+[m[32masserted.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mAsserts:[m
[32m+[m[32m1. `status == Some(503)`, `title == Some("Service Unavailable")`,[m
[32m+[m[32m   `detail == Some("upstream timed out")` — populated correctly.[m
[32m+[m[32m2. `problem_type.is_none()`, `instance.is_none()` — optional fields[m
[32m+[m[32m   default to `None` as documented.[m
[32m+[m[32m3. JSON wire format omits both `"type"` and `"instance"` — i.e., the[m
[32m+[m[32m   `skip_serializing_if = "Option::is_none"` behavior holds for the[m
[32m+[m[32m   constructor's defaults.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### 5. `rfc7807::tests::problem_json_wire_format_with_all_fields`[m
[32m+[m[32m**File:** `pheno-errors/src/rfc7807.rs:329-366`[m
[32m+[m[32m**Closes:** `Problem` serde rename + full positive-case wire format[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mNo previous test exercised the **serde rename** (`#[serde(rename = "type")]`[m
[32m+[m[32mat `rfc7807.rs:57`) in a positive case. The existing[m
[32m+[m[32m`none_fields_are_omitted_from_json` (`rfc7807.rs:254-267`) only checks[m
[32m+[m[32mthat `None` fields are skipped, not that a populated `problem_type`[m
[32m+[m[32mserialises as `"type"` (the RFC 7807 §3.1 mandated key). A refactor that[m
[32m+[m[32mremoved the rename would not be caught.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mAsserts:[m
[32m+[m[32m1. `json.contains("\"type\":\"https://errors.pheno.dev/not-found\"")` —[m
[32m+[m[32m   the rename works.[m
[32m+[m[32m2. `!json.contains("problem_type")` — no Rust field name leaks through.[m
[32m+[m[32m3. All 5 spec fields present in the wire format: `type`, `title`,[m
[32m+[m[32m   `status`, `detail`, `instance`.[m
[32m+[m[32m4. The wire format is itself valid JSON (re-parsed via[m
[32m+[m[32m   `serde_json::from_str::<serde_json::Value>`) and the values match.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m## Before / after count[m

[32m+[m[32m## Cargo.toml change[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mOne line added: `serde_json = "1"` to `[dev-dependencies]`.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mThis was a **pre-existing missing dev-dependency** that blocked test[m
[32m+[m[32mcompilation — the existing tests in `rfc7807` already called[m
[32m+[m[32m`serde_json::to_string(...)` but `serde_json` was not declared. The[m
[32m+[m[32mupstream tests worked anyway only because `serde` (with `derive`)[m
[32m+[m[32mtransitively pulls in some serialization types but not the JSON[m
[32m+[m[32mserialization crate itself. Without this fix, the new wire-format tests[m
[32m+[m[32mwould not have compiled either.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m## Why these 5 (selection rationale)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mThe audit was path-driven: enumerate every public function and[m
[32m+[m[32m`From` branch in `src/lib.rs` and `src/rfc7807.rs`, then check whether[m
[32m+[m[32mthe **observable side-effect** (not just the return value) was[m
[32m+[m[32masserted. Each of the 5 chosen paths has the same structural gap:[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m| Gap pattern                                                           | Found in                |[m
[32m+[m[32m|-----------------------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------|[m
[32m+[m[32m| Return value asserted but side-effect not                             | Tests 1, 2              |[m
[32m+[m[32m| Branch taken but specific field never read                            | Test 3                  |[m
[32m+[m[32m| Constructor only tested in chained form, defaults never asserted      | Test 4                  |[m
[32m+[m[32m| Serde rename never asserted positive; only omission was tested        | Test 5                  |[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mOther functions (constructors, `From` impls for `io::Error` / `&str` /[m
[32m+[m[32m`String` / `anyhow::Error`, `kind()`, `Default for Problem`, `Display`)[m
[32m+[m[32mwere already exercised by the existing 20 tests, so they are not in[m
[32m+[m[32mscope here.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m## Caveats / known issues[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m- **`cargo test -p pheno-errors` (without `--lib`) still fails** due[m
[32m+[m[32m  to 5 pre-existing compile errors in `examples/otel_quickstart.rs`[m
[32m+[m[32m  that reference types and methods that don't exist on `AppError`[m
[32m+[m[32m  (`ErrorContext`, `with_context`, `From<ParseIntError>`). These errors[m
[32m+[m[32m  pre-date this change (the example was committed broken) and are[m
[32m+[m[32m  unrelated to test coverage. Tracked separately.[m
[32m+[m[32m- **Branch not pushed.** Per task directive: "DO NOT push."[m
[32m+[m

[32m+[m[32m# SIDE-04: Cargo.toml Version Alignment Audit (2026-06-21)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Scope:** Audit the 5 pheno-* repos at the monorepo root (`pheno-otel/`, `pheno-port-adapter/`, `pheno-errors/`, `pheno-context/`, `pheno-config/`) for *internal* dep version alignment: i.e. when a `Cargo.toml` declares `pheno-X = "0.4.0"` (or `{ path = "...", version = "0.4.0" }`), does the actual source `pheno-X/Cargo.toml` `[package].version` match? Method: read each repo's `Cargo.toml` + `cargo tree -p <repo>` + `Cargo.lock` cross-check.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m## TL;DR[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m| Repo | Has Cargo.toml? | Source `version` | Internal pheno-* deps declared | Version-pin present? | Mismatches found |[m
[32m+[m[32m|------|-----------------|------------------|--------------------------------|------------------------|------------------|[m
[32m+[m[32m| `pheno-otel`        | **YES** | `0.1.0` (`pheno-otel/Cargo.toml:3`)          | 0 (leaf substrate) | n/a | **0** |[m
[32m+[m[32m| `pheno-port-adapter`| **YES** | `0.1.0` (`pheno-port-adapter/Cargo.toml:3`)  | 1 (`pheno-otel`)   | NO (`path`-only) | **0** |[m
[32m+[m[32m| `pheno-errors`      | **YES** | `0.1.0` (`pheno-errors/Cargo.toml:3`)        | 1 (`pheno-otel`)   | NO (`path`-only) | **0** |[m
[32m+[m[32m| `pheno-context`     | **NO**  | n/a                                           | n/a (no manifest)  | n/a | **STRUCTURAL** (see §3) |[m
[32m+[m[32m| `pheno-config`      | **NO**  | n/a                                           | n/a (no manifest)  | n/a | **STRUCTURAL** (see §4) |[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Headline finding (version alignment):** Of the 5 repos in scope, **3 carry a `Cargo.toml`** and **2 do not** (they are scaffold-state directories with only `docs/`, `i18n/`, and `src/*.rs` files but no manifest). Of the 3 with a manifest, **0 declare a version pin on the one internal pheno-* dep they reference** — both `pheno-port-adapter` and `pheno-errors` use bare `path = "../pheno-otel"` (no `version =` clause). With path-only deps, cargo resolves to whatever the source crate's `[package].version` declares (here, `0.1.0` everywhere), so the structural mismatch count is **0 by design**. The audit's "version-pin drift" dimension is **vacuous**: there is nothing to drift.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Headline finding (structural):** 2 of 5 repos (`pheno-context`, `pheno-config`) have **no `Cargo.toml` at the monorepo root** — they exist only as `src/*.rs` source fragments. The "real" crate for both lives under `FocalPoint/...` per SIDE-01's prior audit (ADR-038 substrate-canonical placement). The root-level `pheno-config/src/secrets.rs` and `pheno-context/src/oidc.rs` use external crates (`zeroize`, `serde`, `tokio`, `figment`, `toml`) that **have no manifest to declare them in**. They cannot be built as a standalone crate at this path.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m## Method[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m1. **Locate each repo:** `ls -la pheno-<name>/` (all 5 dirs confirmed at monorepo root).[m
[32m+[m[32m2. **Read each `Cargo.toml`:** `[package].version` + `[dependencies]` (filter for `pheno-*` entries).[m
[32m+[m[32m3. **For each `pheno-*` dep declared**, locate the source crate's `Cargo.toml` and read its `[package].version`.[m
[32m+[m[32m4. **Run `cargo tree -p <repo>`** for each manifest-bearing repo to get the resolved dep graph.[m
[32m+[m[32m5. **Cross-check `Cargo.lock`** for the resolved version cargo actually locked.[m
[32m+[m[32m6. **Diff** declared-version-pin vs. resolved-version.[m
[32m+[m

[32m+[m[32m#### `cargo tree -p pheno-context` and `cargo tree -p pheno-config`[m
[32m+[m[32mBoth **fail** with:[m
[32m+[m[32m```[m

[32m+[m[32m→ confirms no manifest at root; cargo cannot construct a dep graph for these paths.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m## Per-repo findings[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### 1. `pheno-otel` — v0.1.0, no internal pheno-* deps[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m| Declared dep | Source version | Resolved version (`cargo tree`) | `Cargo.lock` lock version | Mismatch? |[m
[32m+[m[32m|--------------|----------------|---------------------------------|---------------------------|-----------|[m
[32m+[m[32m| (none — leaf substrate) | — | — | — | n/a |[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m- **Source manifest:** `pheno-otel/Cargo.toml:2-3` declares `name = "pheno-otel"`, `version = "0.1.0"`.[m
[32m+[m[32m- **External deps:** `thiserror = "2"`, `serde = { version = "1.0", features = ["derive"] }`, `serde_json = "1.0"` (`pheno-otel/Cargo.toml:25-28`). All external; no fleet-substrate pins.[m
[32m+[m[32m- **No internal pheno-* dep declared.** Cannot drift on the alignment dimension.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Verdict: 0 mismatches.** The substrate is a sink, not a source of cross-crate references.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### 2. `pheno-port-adapter` — v0.1.0, depends on `pheno-otel`[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m| Declared dep | Declaration (Cargo.toml) | Source version of dep | Resolved by cargo | Mismatch? |[m
[32m+[m[32m|--------------|--------------------------|------------------------|--------------------|-----------|[m
[32m+[m[32m| `pheno-otel` | `pheno-otel = { path = "../pheno-otel" }` (line 30) — **no `version =` clause** | `0.1.0` (`pheno-otel/Cargo.toml:3`) | `0.1.0` (path-only → resolves to source) | **0** |[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m- **Source manifest:** `pheno-port-adapter/Cargo.toml:2-3` declares `version = "0.1.0"`.[m
[32m+[m[32m- **Internal dep declared (1):** `pheno-otel` via bare path (`pheno-port-adapter/Cargo.toml:30`); no version pin.[m
[32m+[m[32m- **Cross-check via `Cargo.lock:362-368`:** `pheno-otel` locked at `0.1.0` (path source, no registry source line — confirms workspace/path resolution).[m
[32m+[m[32m- **Cross-check via `cargo tree -p pheno-port-adapter`:** resolves to `pheno-otel v0.1.0 (/Users/.../repos/pheno-otel)`.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Verdict: 0 mismatches.** Path-only dep cannot drift because there is no version pin to drift from; cargo resolves to whatever the source's `[package].version` is.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### 3. `pheno-errors` — v0.1.0, depends on `pheno-otel`[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m| Declared dep | Declaration (Cargo.toml) | Source version of dep | Resolved by cargo | Mismatch? |[m
[32m+[m[32m|--------------|--------------------------|------------------------|--------------------|-----------|[m
[32m+[m[32m| `pheno-otel` | `pheno-otel = { path = "../pheno-otel" }` (line 17) — **no `version =` clause** | `0.1.0` (`pheno-otel/Cargo.toml:3`) | `0.1.0` (path-only → resolves to source) | **0** |[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m- **Source manifest:** `pheno-errors/Cargo.toml:2-3` declares `version = "0.1.0"`.[m
[32m+[m[32m- **Internal dep declared (1):** `pheno-otel` via bare path (`pheno-errors/Cargo.toml:17`); no version pin.[m
[32m+[m[32m- **Cross-check via `Cargo.lock:181-188`:** `pheno-otel` locked at `0.1.0` (path source).[m
[32m+[m[32m- **Cross-check via `cargo tree -p pheno-errors`:** resolves to `pheno-otel v0.1.0 (/Users/.../repos/pheno-otel)`.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Verdict: 0 mismatches.** Same pattern as `pheno-port-adapter`.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### 4. `pheno-context` — STRUCTURAL: no `Cargo.toml` at root[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**No `Cargo.toml` exists at this path.** The directory contains only:[m
[32m+[m[32m- `docs/HEXAGONAL_PORTS.md` (38 lines, the hexagonal-ports adoption notice — v17 T4)[m
[32m+[m[32m- `src/oidc.rs` (229 lines, an OIDC federation reference client per ADR-079; this is the v19 T3 stub)[m
[32m+[m[32m- No `[package]`, no `[dependencies]`, no `Cargo.lock`.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**`cargo tree -p pheno-context` fails** with `error: could not find Cargo.toml`. There is no dep graph to compare.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**`src/oidc.rs` import surface (uncompilable as-is, since no manifest declares the deps):**[m
[32m+[m[32m| Import | External crate needed | Declared in any Cargo.toml? |[m
[32m+[m[32m|--------|----------------------|------------------------------|[m
[32m+[m[32m| `use serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};` (line 10) | `serde` | **No** (no manifest) |[m
[32m+[m[32m| `use tokio::sync::RwLock;` (line 11) | `tokio` | **No** (no manifest) |[m
[32m+[m[32m| `use zeroize::Zeroize;` (line 12) | `zeroize` | **No** (no manifest) |[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mThe header comment on `src/oidc.rs:1-4` says: *"Deps: zeroize, serde, tokio (parent Cargo.toml; not modified here)."* — confirming the author knew the deps belong in a parent manifest, but the parent manifest **does not exist** at the monorepo root.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Canonical home (per SIDE-01 audit):** `FocalPoint/pheno-context/Cargo.toml` (workspace member; `publish = false`). That manifest declares `thiserror = { workspace = true }`, `http = "1.1"`, `dev-dependencies: http = "1.1"`. **It does NOT declare `pheno-otel`, `pheno-errors`, `pheno-port-adapter`, `pheno-config`, `serde`, `tokio`, or `zeroize` either** — so even the canonical home is out of sync with the root-level `src/oidc.rs` content. This is a *separate* drift between source content and the canonical manifest, not the version-alignment kind SIDE-04 is about, but it is the same family of issue.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Verdict: STRUCTURAL FINDING, not a version-alignment mismatch.** The "real" question — does the version pin in some (hypothetical) `pheno-context/Cargo.toml` match? — is moot because no manifest exists. The applicable finding is: "this directory cannot be built as a standalone crate; the source content references external crates with no manifest to resolve them."[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### 5. `pheno-config` — STRUCTURAL: no `Cargo.toml` at root[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**No `Cargo.toml` exists at this path.** The directory contains:[m
[32m+[m[32m- `docs/HEXAGONAL_PORTS.md` (36 lines, hexagonal-ports adoption notice — v17 T4)[m
[32m+[m[32m- `docs/architecture/pheno-config.md` (122 lines, C4 container + cascade-sequence diagrams)[m
[32m+[m[32m- `i18n/{en,es,ja}/pheno-config.ftl` (3 locale files, no Rust code)[m
[32m+[m[32m- `src/cascade.rs` (93 lines, the Figment-based config-cascade substrate per ADR-022)[m
[32m+[m[32m- `src/secrets.rs` (59 lines, the zeroize-based secret-holding wrapper per ADR-078 / v19 T2)[m
[32m+[m[32m- `tests/cascade_test.rs` (mentioned by the architecture doc but not present at this path)[m
[32m+[m[32m- No `[package]`, no `[dependencies]`, no `Cargo.lock`.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**`cargo tree -p pheno-config` fails** with `error: could not find Cargo.toml`. There is no dep graph to compare.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**`src/cascade.rs` import surface (uncompilable as-is, since no manifest declares the deps):**[m
[32m+[m[32m| Import | External crate needed | Declared in any Cargo.toml at this path? |[m
[32m+[m[32m|--------|----------------------|-------------------------------------------|[m
[32m+[m[32m| `use figment::providers::{Env, Format, Jetbrains, Toml};` (line 23-25) | `figment` | **No** (no manifest) |[m
[32m+[m[32m| `use figment::Figment;` (line 25) | `figment` | **No** (no manifest) |[m
[32m+[m[32m| `toml::Value` in test (line 88) | `toml` | **No** (no manifest) |[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**`src/secrets.rs` import surface:**[m
[32m+[m[32m| Import | External crate needed | Declared? |[m
[32m+[m[32m|--------|----------------------|-----------|[m
[32m+[m[32m| `use zeroize::{Zeroize, ZeroizeOnDrop};` (line 15) | `zeroize` | **No** (no manifest) |[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Canonical home (per SIDE-01 audit):** Two candidates exist for the "real" `pheno-config` crate:[m
[32m+[m[32m1. `FocalPoint/pheno-config/Cargo.toml` (workspace member; `publish = false`); declared deps: `figment = { version = "0.10", features = ["toml", "env"] }`, `serde = "1"`, `thiserror = "1"`, `pheno-errors = "0.1"`, dev-deps: `pheno-tracing`, `pheno-port-adapter`. **This is the canonical substrate per SIDE-01 and ADR-022.**[m
[32m+[m[32m2. `Configra/crates/pheno-config/Cargo.toml` (per ADR-031, Configra is the **canonical repo name** for config; this is where new config work should land going forward).[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mNeither of these is the same path as the monorepo-root `pheno-config/` directory. The root-level `pheno-config/src/cascade.rs` and `src/secrets.rs` are **source fragments that were inlined at root** (likely as part of a v17/v19 track) but never wrapped in a manifest.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Verdict: STRUCTURAL FINDING, not a version-alignment mismatch.** Same shape as `pheno-context`. Cannot be built as a standalone crate; source content references external crates (`figment`, `toml`, `zeroize`) with no manifest to resolve them.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m

[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m| From (consumer) | To (dep) | Declaration form | Version requested | Source `[package].version` of dep | Resolved by cargo | Locked in `Cargo.lock` | Drifted? |[m
[32m+[m[32m|-----------------|----------|------------------|-------------------|----------------------------------|-------------------|------------------------|----------|[m
[32m+[m[32m| `pheno-otel`        | (none — leaf)            | n/a        | n/a    | n/a    | n/a    | n/a    | n/a |[m
[32m+[m[32m| `pheno-port-adapter` | `pheno-otel`            | `path`-only | —      | `0.1.0` | `0.1.0` | `0.1.0` | **No** |[m
[32m+[m[32m| `pheno-errors`       | `pheno-otel`            | `path`-only | —      | `0.1.0` | `0.1.0` | `0.1.0` | **No** |[m

[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Total version-alignment mismatches: 0.**[m
[32m+[m[32m**Total structural "no Cargo.toml" findings: 2** (`pheno-context`, `pheno-config`).[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m## Cross-check vs. SIDE-01 (2026-06-21, earlier same-day audit)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mSIDE-01 audited the same 6 crates for **crates.io publication status** and found:[m
[32m+[m[32m- All 6 declare `version = "0.1.0"` in their primary manifest.[m
[32m+[m[32m- None are published to crates.io.[m
[32m+[m[32m- All internal pheno-* deps use `path = "..."` or `workspace = true` — zero SemVer pins exist anywhere.[m
[32m+[m[32m- → "the audit's stated goal (list crates where current < latest) returns 0 actionable items, because there is no `latest` to compare against."[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mSIDE-04 audits the **internal alignment** dimension (does the version in dep A's Cargo.toml match the source of dep B?) and arrives at the same conclusion by a different route:[m
[32m+[m[32m- 3 of the 5 in-scope repos have a manifest; 2 do not.[m
[32m+[m[32m- The 3 manifests collectively declare **2 internal pheno-* references** (both `pheno-otel`, both bare `path`).[m
[32m+[m[32m- Both references are unpinned → resolution is structural (source-version) → cannot drift.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Combined SIDE-01 + SIDE-04 verdict:** The 5 in-scope crates have a version-alignment posture that is **structurally drift-proof** (path-only, no pins) **but not structurally sound** (2 of 5 lack a manifest entirely). The "alignment" question has a vacuous "yes" answer for the 3 buildable repos; the more pressing question — *"should these 5 repos even be top-level crates?"* — is the structural concern that ADR-031 (Configra absorb) and ADR-038 (hex-port L4) are already answering in the substrate-canonical-homes direction.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m## Findings (numbered, with severity)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m1. **F-1 (Informational):** Zero version-alignment mismatches across the 3 manifest-bearing repos (`pheno-otel`, `pheno-port-adapter`, `pheno-errors`). Both internal pheno-* references are bare `path` deps and resolve cleanly to the source's `[package].version = "0.1.0"`.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m2. **F-2 (P2 — Structural):** `pheno-context/` at the monorepo root has no `Cargo.toml`. It contains `src/oidc.rs` (a v19 T3 OIDC reference client per ADR-079) that imports `serde`, `tokio`, and `zeroize`, none of which are declared. The crate cannot be built from this path. The canonical home (`FocalPoint/pheno-context/Cargo.toml` per SIDE-01) does not currently declare these deps either — so the `src/oidc.rs` content is in transit between scaffolds and is not aligned with any active manifest.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m3. **F-3 (P2 — Structural):** `pheno-config/` at the monorepo root has no `Cargo.toml`. It contains `src/cascade.rs` (Figment cascade per ADR-022) and `src/secrets.rs` (zeroize wrapper per ADR-078), both of which import external crates (`figment`, `toml`, `zeroize`) that are undeclared. The crate cannot be built from this path. The canonical homes (`FocalPoint/pheno-config/Cargo.toml`, `Configra/crates/pheno-config/Cargo.toml`) are separate from this root-level directory; the root-level source fragments have no manifest binding them.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m4. **F-4 (P3 — Documentation drift, out of strict scope):** The header comment in `pheno-context/src/oidc.rs:1-4` says *"Deps: zeroize, serde, tokio (parent Cargo.toml; not modified here)"* — confirming the author knew the parent manifest was supposed to exist. It does not. This is a non-actionable-but-noteworthy documentation-vs-reality drift.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m5. **F-5 (P3 — Reproducibility note, repeats SIDE-01 §4):** With path-only deps, switching to `pheno-otel = { path = "../pheno-otel", version = "0.1.0" }` would not change resolution today (the source IS `0.1.0`) but would catch future drift if the source bumps. Worth adding as a hygiene pass once v19 T2/T3 land.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m## Recommendations (in order of urgency)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### R-1 (resolve F-2 + F-3) — Decide the fate of root-level `pheno-context/` and `pheno-config/`[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mThree options; pick one per repo:[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m| Option | What | Trade-off |[m
[32m+[m[32m|--------|------|-----------|[m
[32m+[m[32m| **(a) Move to canonical home** | `git mv pheno-context/src/oidc.rs FocalPoint/pheno-context/src/oidc.rs` (and update `FocalPoint/pheno-context/Cargo.toml` to add `tokio`, `serde`, `zeroize` deps for it). Same for `pheno-config/src/cascade.rs` and `src/secrets.rs` → `FocalPoint/pheno-config/src/` (or `Configra/crates/pheno-config/src/` per ADR-031). | Cleanest. Aligns with SIDE-01's canonical-home guidance and ADR-031's Configra absorb. |[m
[32m+[m[32m| **(b) Add a manifest at root** | Author a `pheno-context/Cargo.toml` + `pheno-config/Cargo.toml` at the monorepo root that declares the deps referenced by the source files. | Duplicates the canonical home. Inverts the ADR-022/031/038 substrate-placement direction. **Not recommended** unless there's a reason these specific fragments must be siblings to other root-level crates. |[m
[32m+[m[32m| **(c) Delete the root-level fragments** | If the source content is already replicated at the canonical home, just delete the root-level `pheno-context/` and `pheno-config/` directories. | Cleanest *if* the canonical home already has equivalent content. Worth checking first: does `FocalPoint/pheno-config/src/cascade.rs` exist? Does it have the same `build_cascade()` shape? If yes, the root-level `pheno-config/src/cascade.rs` is redundant. |[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Recommendation:** **R-1 (a) — move to canonical home, for both repos.** This is the path the rest of the fleet is already on (per SIDE-01 + ADR-022/031/038). The root-level `pheno-context/` and `pheno-config/` directories look like staging areas that were never wrapped in manifests; the v19 plan already routes new config/context work to `Configra` (ADR-031) and the existing substrate (per `focalpoint-wt-v12-16-17/pheno-config/Cargo.toml` which IS a manifest), so the right move is to consolidate, not to add new manifests.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### R-2 (hygiene, low priority) — Add `version = "0.1.0"` to the two `pheno-otel` path-deps[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mTrivial change to `pheno-port-adapter/Cargo.toml:30` and `pheno-errors/Cargo.toml:17`:[m
[32m+[m[32m```toml[m
[32m+[m[32mpheno-otel = { path = "../pheno-otel", version = "0.1.0" }[m
[32m+[m[32m```[m
[32m+[m[32mToday this changes nothing (source IS `0.1.0`). It is **defensive** against future drift if `pheno-otel` bumps to `0.2.0` without a coordinated update to the consumers' `Cargo.toml`. F-5's reproducibility note. P3.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### R-3 (out of scope but flagged) — Decide if `pheno-context` should grow a `Cargo.toml` at all[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m`pheno-context/docs/HEXAGONAL_PORTS.md:10-14` describes `pheno-context` as *"the canonical `Context` carrier (request id, span id, trace id, user/org metadata, extensible key-value bag) and a `ContextBuilder`"* — i.e. a pure value type. The current `src/oidc.rs` content is **OIDC**, not context — it's the v19 T3 stub (per ADR-079). So `pheno-context` is conflating two substrate roles:[m
[32m+[m[32m- (a) The original "request context carrier" (FocalPoint home)[m
[32m+[m[32m- (b) The v19 OIDC federation client (per ADR-079 / `plans/2026-06-21-v19-71-pillar-cycle-9-p0.md §2 T3`)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mThese should live in different crates. Recommend R-1a for the OIDC code (move to a new `pheno-oidc` substrate or to `pheno-context/src/oidc.rs` at the FocalPoint canonical home, with the OIDC deps added to that manifest). This is a v19+ decision and out of scope for the immediate SIDE-04 audit, but the version-alignment audit surfaces it.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m

[32m+[m[32m "serde_json",[m
[32m+[m[32m "thiserror",[m
[32m+[m[32m "tracing",[m
[32m+[m[32m "tracing-test",[m
[32m+[m[32m][m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m[[package]][m
[32m+[m[32mname = "pheno-otel"[m
[32m+[m[32mversion = "0.1.0"[m
[32m+[m[32mdependencies = [[m
[32m+[m[32m "serde",[m

[32m+[m[32m "thiserror",[m
[32m+[m[32m][m

[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**`pheno-otel/Cargo.lock:18-24`**[m
[32m+[m[32m```toml[m
[32m+[m[32m[[package]][m
[32m+[m[32mname = "pheno-otel"[m
[32m+[m[32mversion = "0.1.0"[m
[32m+[m[32mdependencies = [[m
[32m+[m[32m "serde",[m

[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mAll three `Cargo.lock` files agree: `pheno-otel` is locked at `0.1.0`, with no registry source line (path-only resolution). All source `[package].version` declarations are `0.1.0`. No drift.[m
[32m+[m

[32m+[m[32m### A.4 — Cross-check: `focalpoint-wt-v12-16-17/` mirror state (informational, not in scope)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mThe `focalpoint-wt-v12-16-17` worktree (a worktree-of-a-worktree per the project conventions) carries **older / divergent** copies of all 5 crates:[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m| Crate | `repos/<name>/Cargo.toml` (current) | `focalpoint-wt-v12-16-17/<name>/Cargo.toml` (older) |[m
[32m+[m[32m|-------|-------------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------|[m
[32m+[m[32m| `pheno-otel`         | v0.1.0, deps: thiserror/serde/serde_json | v0.1.0, deps: opentelemetry 0.27 + otlp 0.27 + thiserror |[m
[32m+[m[32m| `pheno-port-adapter` | v0.1.0, deps: thiserror/tokio/async-trait/redis/pheno-otel | v0.1.0, deps: thiserror only (no pheno-otel) |[m
[32m+[m[32m| `pheno-errors`       | v0.1.0, deps: anyhow/thiserror/tracing/serde/**pheno-otel** | v0.1.0, deps: thiserror/anyhow/tracing (no pheno-otel) |[m
[32m+[m[32m| `pheno-config`       | NO Cargo.toml                          | v0.1.0, deps: thiserror/serde/serde_json |[m
[32m+[m[32m| `pheno-context`      | NO Cargo.toml                          | v0.1.0, deps: thiserror/http |[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mThis confirms the v17/v18/v19 wave work: the root-level `pheno-otel`, `pheno-port-adapter`, `pheno-errors` are the **post-OTLP-substrate** versions (per ADR-037), while the worktree mirror is the **pre-OTLP-substrate** versions. The structural absence of `pheno-config` and `pheno-context` manifests at root aligns with the substrate-canonical-homes migration (ADR-031 → Configra for config; ADR-038 → FocalPoint workspace for context-hexagonal-ports).[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mThis is **not a version-alignment mismatch** in the strict SIDE-04 sense (different paths, different worktrees, different points in time) but is corroborating evidence that the root-level `pheno-config/` and `pheno-context/` are **intentionally scaffold-state**, awaiting either a manifest or a move to canonical home.[m
[32m+[m

[32m+[m[32m**Cross-references:** SIDE-01 (`findings/2026-06-21-SIDE-01-dep-audit.md`) covers the crates.io-publication dimension. This doc (SIDE-04) covers the internal dep version-alignment dimension. Both reach the same zero-drift conclusion via different routes.[m

[32m+[m[32m# SIDE-10 — Async Runtime Consistency Across the pheno-* Rust Fleet[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Date:** 2026-06-21 (PDT)[m
[32m+[m[32m**Author:** orchestrator (v19 cycle-9 P1 sweep)[m
[32m+[m[32m**Status:** COMPLETE — 5/5 repos audited[m
[32m+[m[32m**Track:** SIDE-10 (cross-cutting)[m
[32m+[m[32m**Related:** v17 T6 / L10 async runtime decision (ADR-088 planned); v19 cycle-9 P1 reduction wave[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m> **Snapshot note (important).** This audit was performed against the working tree on 2026-06-21 between 13:30-13:50 PDT. During the audit window, several pheno-* subdirectories changed state (e.g. `pheno-context/` appeared, then disappeared; `pheno-config/` gained a `Cargo.lock` and `src/`). Where a file was present at audit time and absent at write time, this is noted in § 3 and § 8. All line citations below were re-verified against the working tree at 2026-06-21 13:50 PDT before publishing.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m## 1. Executive Summary[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mThe pheno-* Rust fleet is **100 % tokio** (for the 2 repos that need an async runtime). No `async-std` and no `smol` usage was found in any of the 5 audited repos or in the wider `pheno-*` source tree (full sweep, see § 5). This validates the v17 T6 / L10 decision (`plans/2026-06-21-v17-71-pillar-cycle-7-p0.md:43-45`) that named tokio as the existing precedent and target runtime.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Per-repo runtime summary (5 repos):**[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m| # | Repo | Async runtime | Lock-resolved version | Feature policy | MSRV | Cargo.toml in cone? |[m
[32m+[m[32m|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|[m
[32m+[m[32m| 1 | `pheno-errors` | **none (sync)** | n/a | n/a | **unspecified** | yes |[m
[32m+[m[32m| 2 | `pheno-otel` | **none (sync)** | n/a | n/a | 1.75 | yes |[m
[32m+[m[32m| 3 | `pheno-config` | **none (sync)** | n/a (lock shows only `zeroize 1.9.0`) | n/a | unspecified (no Cargo.toml in cone) | **no (Cargo.lock only)** |[m
[32m+[m[32m| 4 | `pheno-port-adapter` | **tokio** | **1.52.3** | minimal (`rt-multi-thread, macros, sync, time`) | 1.82 | yes |[m
[32m+[m[32m| 5 | `pheno-tracing` | **tokio** | **1.52.3** | `full` | 1.75 | yes |[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Headline findings:**[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m- **F-1 (positive):** Both async-using repos converge on tokio. No fragmentation. ADR-088's target is already met.[m
[32m+[m[32m- **F-2 (mismatch):** tokio feature-flag policy diverges between `pheno-port-adapter` (minimal: `rt-multi-thread, macros, sync, time`) and `pheno-tracing` (`full`). Both work, but the divergence is unjustified.[m
[32m+[m[32m- **F-3 (gap):** `pheno-config` exists with `src/`, `tests/`, `Cargo.lock`, but its `Cargo.toml` is absent from this branch's sparse-checkout cone. Verifiability gap (cannot confirm MSRV or declared feature sets).[m
[32m+[m[32m- **F-4 (gap):** The v17 T6 ADR doc (`docs/architecture/async-runtime-decision.md`) was approved in plan (`plans/2026-06-21-v17-71-pillar-cycle-7-p0.md:43-45`) but was never authored. This SIDE-10 doubles as the formal record.[m
[32m+[m[32m- **F-5 (positive):** Lock-resolved tokio versions are identical (1.52.3) for both repos with lock files. `async-trait` is also identical (0.1.89). No patch-version drift.[m
[32m+[m[32m- **F-6 (gap):** No fleet-wide policy banning `async-std` / `smol` from `pheno-*` Cargo.toml. The 100 % tokio adoption is convention, not enforcement.[m
[32m+[m[32m- **F-7 (mismatch):** MSRV floor is divergent — `pheno-port-adapter` requires 1.82, `pheno-otel` and `pheno-tracing` require 1.75, `pheno-errors` and `pheno-config` declare no MSRV.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m## 2. Methodology[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mFor each of the 5 repos:[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m1. Read `Cargo.toml` (when present in the sparse-checkout cone) and capture declared async-runtime deps, feature flags, and MSRV.[m
[32m+[m[32m2. Read `Cargo.lock` (when present) and record the lock-resolved version.[m
[32m+[m[32m3. Scan `src/**/*.rs` and `tests/**/*.rs` for `use tokio`, `use async_std`, `use smol`, `use async_trait`, `async fn`, `.await`, `#[tokio::test]`, etc.[m
[32m+[m[32m4. Note any declared but unused or used but undeclared runtime.[m
[32m+[m[32m5. Cross-reference v17 T6 plan and any sibling ADRs.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mSparse-checkout cone for this branch (sparse-checkout cone-mode is `true`, see AGENTS.md "Stale / warnings"): excludes the actual `Cargo.toml` for `pheno-config`, `pheno-context`, and `pheno-flags`. The audit compensates by reading source files and any available `Cargo.lock`. A previous version of this draft used `pheno-context/src/oidc.rs` as the 5th repo's source of truth; that file disappeared from the working tree mid-audit (the v19 T3 OIDC federation track work landed and replaced it with a synchronous `parking_lot::RwLock`-based implementation in `FocalPoint/pheno-context/src/oidc.rs`). The 5th repo in this final draft is `pheno-config`, whose `Cargo.lock` is in the cone and whose `src/` tree shows zero async usage.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m## 3. Per-Repo Findings[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### 3.1 pheno-errors[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**File:** `pheno-errors/Cargo.toml`[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m- Async runtime: **none** (sync only).[m
[32m+[m[32m- Declared deps (`pheno-errors/Cargo.toml:9-17`):[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `anyhow = "1"` (`pheno-errors/Cargo.toml:10`)[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `thiserror = "2"` (`pheno-errors/Cargo.toml:11`)[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `tracing = "0.1"` (`pheno-errors/Cargo.toml:12`)[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `serde = { version = "1", features = ["derive"] }` (`pheno-errors/Cargo.toml:13`)[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `pheno-otel = { path = "../pheno-otel" }` (`pheno-errors/Cargo.toml:17`)[m
[32m+[m[32m- Dev-deps (`pheno-errors/Cargo.toml:19-21`):[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `proptest = "1"` (`pheno-errors/Cargo.toml:20`)[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `tracing-test = "0.2"` (`pheno-errors/Cargo.toml:21`)[m
[32m+[m[32m- MSRV: **not declared** (no `rust-version` field anywhere in the file).[m
[32m+[m[32m- Sync-only by design: pure error-substrate crate that consolidates 5 common error patterns into a single `AppError` type. No I/O, no async calls.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Verdict:** No change needed. A substrate error crate should not depend on a runtime; staying sync keeps it usable from tokio, async-std, smol, and sync contexts alike.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### 3.2 pheno-otel[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**File:** `pheno-otel/Cargo.toml`[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m- Async runtime: **none** (sync only).[m
[32m+[m[32m- Declared deps (`pheno-otel/Cargo.toml:24-26`):[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `thiserror = "2"`[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `serde = { version = "1.0", features = ["derive"] }`[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `serde_json = "1.0"`[m
[32m+[m[32m- Dev-deps: empty (per comment: "Reserved for OTLP smoke test fixtures").[m
[32m+[m[32m- MSRV: 1.75 (`pheno-otel/Cargo.toml:5`).[m
[32m+[m[32m- Sync-only by design: pure wire-format substrate. It serializes OTLP messages to bytes; the *transport* (HTTP/gRPC) is the consumer's responsibility. ADR-037 / substrate-37 explicitly excludes a runtime so the substrate stays runtime-agnostic.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Verdict:** No change needed. Sync wire-format is the right substrate boundary; transport adapters belong in a separate crate (e.g. `pheno-otel-transport` if one is needed).[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Note:** `pheno-otel/Cargo.toml:11` lists `categories = ["development-tools", "api-bindings", "asynchronous"]`. The `asynchronous` category is aspirational (the crate is OTLP-ready, runtime-agnostic); it does not imply a tokio dep. No action needed.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### 3.3 pheno-config[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Files:** `pheno-config/Cargo.lock` (present in cone); `pheno-config/src/cascade.rs`, `pheno-config/src/secrets.rs` (present); `pheno-config/Cargo.toml` **absent from this branch's sparse-checkout cone**.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m- Async runtime: **none** (sync only).[m
[32m+[m[32m- Lock-resolved deps (`pheno-config/Cargo.lock`): the only non-pheno-config package listed is `zeroize 1.9.0`. No tokio, async-trait, async-std, smol, or futures anywhere in the lock.[m
[32m+[m[32m- Source usage scan (`pheno-config/src/*.rs`, `pheno-config/tests/*.rs`): zero matches for `use tokio`, `async fn`, `.await`, `#[tokio::test]`, `async-trait`, `async_std`, `smol`. Only matches were `#[test]` (4 instances in `cascade.rs` / `secrets.rs`).[m
[32m+[m[32m- MSRV: **unknown** — no Cargo.toml in cone to inspect.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Verdict:** sync, no async deps. Adding `Cargo.toml` to the sparse-checkout cone is the only outstanding action; no async consistency work needed in the crate itself.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### 3.4 pheno-port-adapter[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**File:** `pheno-port-adapter/Cargo.toml`[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m- Async runtime: **tokio** (declared and locked).[m
[32m+[m[32m- Declared deps (`pheno-port-adapter/Cargo.toml:9-30`):[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `thiserror = "2.0"` (`pheno-port-adapter/Cargo.toml:10`)[m
[32m+[m[32m  - **tokio** = `{ version = "1", features = ["rt-multi-thread", "macros", "sync", "time"] }` (`pheno-port-adapter/Cargo.toml:16`)[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `async-trait = "0.1"` (`pheno-port-adapter/Cargo.toml:20`)[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `redis = { version = "0.27", default-features = false, features = ["tokio-comp", "connection-manager"] }` (`pheno-port-adapter/Cargo.toml:24`)[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `pheno-otel = { path = "../pheno-otel" }` (`pheno-port-adapter/Cargo.toml:30`)[m
[32m+[m[32m- Dev-deps (`pheno-port-adapter/Cargo.toml:32-34`):[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `serde_json = "1"` (`pheno-port-adapter/Cargo.toml:33`)[m
[32m+[m[32m  - **dev-deps tokio** = `{ version = "1", features = ["macros", "rt-multi-thread"] }` (`pheno-port-adapter/Cargo.toml:34`)[m
[32m+[m[32m- Cargo.toml comment (`pheno-port-adapter/Cargo.toml:11-15`) explicitly justifies the tokio choice: *"Async runtime backing the hex-port traits (HexCachePort, HexTimePort, ...). Kept as a normal dep (not just dev-deps) because the hex-port adapters return `impl Future` from their `async fn` methods; tokio's macros and runtime are needed at compile time even when callers drive the adapters from a different executor."*[m
[32m+[m[32m- Lock-resolved versions (`pheno-port-adapter/Cargo.lock`):[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `tokio` → **1.52.3**[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `async-trait` → **0.1.89**[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `futures` → **0.3.32** (transitive via `redis 0.27`)[m
[32m+[m[32m- MSRV: **1.82** (`pheno-port-adapter/Cargo.toml:5`).[m
[32m+[m[32m- Fuzz crate (`pheno-port-adapter/fuzz/Cargo.toml`): no tokio — `libfuzzer-sys = "0.4"` only.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Feature-flag analysis:**[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m- Main (`pheno-port-adapter/Cargo.toml:16`): `rt-multi-thread + macros + sync + time`. Does *not* include `rt` explicitly, but `rt-multi-thread` is a superset of `rt`, so the runtime is always available.[m
[32m+[m[32m- Dev (`pheno-port-adapter/Cargo.toml:34`): `macros + rt-multi-thread` only — drops `sync` and `time`. Tests that touch `tokio::sync::*` or `tokio::time::*` would fail to compile. No such test exists today; this is a latent footgun if a future test touches `tokio::sync::RwLock` or `tokio::time::timeout`.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Verdict:** tokio, minimal-feature philosophy. Version-alignment is perfect (1.52.3). The feature split between main and dev-deps is risky (see § 6 R-2).[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### 3.5 pheno-tracing[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**File:** `pheno-tracing/Cargo.toml`[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m- Async runtime: **tokio** (declared and locked).[m
[32m+[m[32m- Declared deps (`pheno-tracing/Cargo.toml:25-38`):[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `async-trait = "0.1"` (`pheno-tracing/Cargo.toml:26`)[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `pheno-otel = { path = "../pheno-otel" }` (`pheno-tracing/Cargo.toml:31`)[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `serde = { version = "1.0", features = ["derive"] }` (`pheno-tracing/Cargo.toml:32`)[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `serde_json = "1.0"` (`pheno-tracing/Cargo.toml:33`)[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `thiserror = "2"` (`pheno-tracing/Cargo.toml:34`)[m
[32m+[m[32m  - **tokio** = `{ version = "1", features = ["full"] }` (`pheno-tracing/Cargo.toml:35`)[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `tracing = "0.1"` (`pheno-tracing/Cargo.toml:36`)[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `tracing-subscriber = { version = "0.3", features = ["env-filter", "fmt", "json"] }` (`pheno-tracing/Cargo.toml:37`)[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `chrono = { version = "0.4", features = ["serde"] }` (`pheno-tracing/Cargo.toml:38`)[m
[32m+[m[32m- Dev-deps (`pheno-tracing/Cargo.toml:40-41`):[m
[32m+[m[32m  - **dev-deps tokio** = `{ version = "1", features = ["rt", "macros", "test-util"] }` (`pheno-tracing/Cargo.toml:41`)[m
[32m+[m[32m- Lock-resolved versions (`pheno-tracing/Cargo.lock`):[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `tokio` → **1.52.3**[m
[32m+[m[32m  - `async-trait` → **0.1.89**[m
[32m+[m[32m- MSRV: **1.75** (`pheno-tracing/Cargo.toml:5`).[m
[32m+[m[32m- Forward-compat shim (`pheno-tracing/Cargo.toml:43-50`): `tracing-0-2 = []` feature, no-op today, gated against `tracing 0.2` GA.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Feature-flag analysis:**[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m- Main (`pheno-tracing/Cargo.toml:35`): `full`. Pulls in every tokio feature, including `fs`, `process`, `signal`, `parking_lot`, etc. — most of which a tracing substrate does not need.[m
[32m+[m[32m- Dev (`pheno-tracing/Cargo.toml:41`): `rt + macros + test-util` — minimal, single-threaded runtime for tests.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Verdict:** tokio, `full` feature philosophy. The `full` feature set inflates compile time and binary size for a substrate whose only tokio surface area is `tokio::spawn` (background flush workers), `tokio::sync::Mutex` (in-memory buffer), and `tokio::time` (debounce timers). Recommend trimming to a minimal explicit set (see § 6 R-1).[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m## 4. Fleet-Wide Consistency Matrix[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m| Dimension | pheno-errors | pheno-otel | pheno-config | pheno-port-adapter | pheno-tracing | Fleet verdict |[m
[32m+[m[32m|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|[m
[32m+[m[32m| **Runtime choice** | sync | sync | sync | tokio | tokio | 100 % tokio (2/2 async repos) |[m
[32m+[m[32m| **tokio version (locked)** | n/a | n/a | n/a | **1.52.3** | **1.52.3** | identical where known |[m
[32m+[m[32m| **tokio version (declared)** | n/a | n/a | n/a | `"1"` | `"1"` | identical where known |[m
[32m+[m[32m| **Feature policy** | n/a | n/a | n/a | minimal | `full` | **divergent (see F-2)** |[m
[32m+[m[32m| **`async-trait`** | n/a | n/a | n/a | `0.1.89` | `0.1.89` | identical where known |[m
[32m+[m[32m| **MSRV** | unspecified | 1.75 | unspecified | **1.82** | 1.75 | **divergent (1.75 vs 1.82, plus 2 unspecified)** |[m
[32m+[m[32m| **`async-std` usage** | none | none | none | none | none | 0/5 |[m
[32m+[m[32m| **`smol` usage** | none | none | none | none | none | 0/5 |[m
[32m+[m[32m| **Cargo.toml in cone?** | yes | yes | **no (lock only)** | yes | yes | sparse-checkout gap |[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**No version mismatches found** between `pheno-port-adapter` and `pheno-tracing`. Both declare `tokio = "1"` and both resolve to `1.52.3`. `async-trait` is identical at `0.1.89`.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Two divergences worth fixing:**[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m1. **Feature policy**: minimal vs `full`. Both work; both compile. The fleet should pick one.[m
[32m+[m[32m2. **MSRV**: 1.75 (`pheno-otel`, `pheno-tracing`) vs 1.82 (`pheno-port-adapter`) vs unspecified (`pheno-errors`, `pheno-config`). The 1.82 floor blocks tokio-version upgrades that might land on a 1.75-only release branch. Align to 1.82 fleet-wide, or document why `pheno-port-adapter` needs the higher floor (likely a `tokio::task::unconstrained` or another 1.80+ feature — needs verification).[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m## 5. async-std / smol Absence — Sweep[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mTo rule out accidental adoption of a competing runtime, the following was verified across the entire `pheno-*` Rust source tree (root + `pheno-config`, `pheno-errors`, `pheno-flags`, `pheno-otel`, `pheno-port-adapter`, `pheno-tracing` — note: `pheno-context/` was empty at the time of this sweep):[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m| Pattern | Files matched | Repos matched |[m
[32m+[m[32m|---|---|---|[m
[32m+[m[32m| `use async_std` / `use async_std::` | 0 | 0/5 |[m
[32m+[m[32m| `use smol` / `use smol::` | 0 | 0/5 |[m
[32m+[m[32m| `async_std =` in any Cargo.toml | 0 | 0/5 |[m
[32m+[m[32m| `smol =` in any Cargo.toml | 0 | 0/5 |[m
[32m+[m[32m| `async-std-runtime` feature on any dep | 0 | 0/5 |[m
[32m+[m[32m| `tokio` (any) | 6 lines | 2/5 (pheno-port-adapter, pheno-tracing) |[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Conclusion:** Zero adoption of `async-std` or `smol` anywhere in the audited fleet. The 100 % tokio stance is intact.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m## 6. Recommendations[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### R-1 (P3 / nice-to-have): Standardize tokio feature-flag policy[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mPick **explicit minimal feature sets** as the fleet default. `full` is a code smell for a substrate — it pulls in tokio components the crate does not need, hurts incremental compile times, and obscures the actual tokio surface area in code review.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Proposed canonical feature set for tokio-using pheno-* substrates:**[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m```toml[m
[32m+[m[32mtokio = { version = "1", features = ["rt-multi-thread", "macros", "sync", "time"] }[m
[32m+[m[32m```[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mThis matches `pheno-port-adapter`'s main-dep choice (`pheno-port-adapter/Cargo.toml:16`) and is the smallest set that supports hex-port adapters (return `impl Future` + drive tests).[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Action:**[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m- Update `pheno-tracing/Cargo.toml:35` to use the minimal explicit set instead of `"full"`. Audit which tokio features `pheno-tracing`'s `src/` actually uses; promote any that are missing.[m
[32m+[m[32m- Add a fleet policy note in `docs/architecture/async-runtime-decision.md` (see R-4) that documents the chosen feature set and the rationale.[m
[32m+[m[32m- Add a CI lint that fails any `pheno-*` Cargo.toml containing `tokio = { version = "1", features = ["full"] }` (allowlist: none).[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### R-2 (P3 / latent footgun): Unify main + dev tokio feature sets[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m`pheno-port-adapter/Cargo.toml:16` and `pheno-port-adapter/Cargo.toml:34` declare different tokio feature sets in `[dependencies]` and `[dev-dependencies]`. The dev-dep set is a strict subset. A test that uses `tokio::sync` or `tokio::time` will fail to compile.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Action:**[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m- Unify both crates' dev-dep tokio features with the main-dep set. Tests should exercise the same surface area the crate ships.[m
[32m+[m[32m- Update `pheno-port-adapter/Cargo.toml:34` to add `"sync", "time"` to the dev-deps tokio feature list.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### R-3 (P3 / hygiene): Fix sparse-checkout cone for pheno-config[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m`pheno-config/` exists with `src/`, `tests/`, and `Cargo.lock` in this branch but contains no `Cargo.toml`. The lock file references `pheno-config 0.1.0` (`pheno-config/Cargo.lock:6-8`) but cannot confirm MSRV or declared feature sets.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Action:**[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m- Update `.git/info/sparse-checkout` to include `pheno-config/Cargo.toml` (and likewise for `pheno-context`, `pheno-flags`, and any other pheno-* Rust repo missing its manifest).[m
[32m+[m[32m- Alternatively, push the audit to verify against `KooshaPari/pheno-config` on GitHub directly.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### R-4 (P3 / governance gap): Author the v17 T6 ADR doc[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mThe v17 plan (`plans/2026-06-21-v17-71-pillar-cycle-7-p0.md:43-45`) approved an ADR at `docs/architecture/async-runtime-decision.md` but the file was never written. This SIDE-10 fills the gap as an audit record, but the formal ADR should still be authored.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Action:**[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m- Create `docs/architecture/async-runtime-decision.md` mirroring the structure of `docs/architecture/hexagonal-ports.md` and `docs/architecture/type-safety-convention.md`. Cite this SIDE-10 as the audit basis.[m
[32m+[m[32m- Number it ADR-088 (per the v17 T6 plan reference).[m
[32m+[m[32m- Promote to `docs/adr/2026-06-21/ADR-088-tokio-canonical-runtime.md` if the file moves to the ADR directory.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### R-5 (P3 / enforcement): Add deny.toml lint for forbidden runtimes[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mNeither `pheno-port-adapter/deny.toml` nor `pheno-tracing/deny.toml` currently bans `async-std` or `smol` as transitive deps. The 100 % tokio stance is convention only.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Action:**[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m- Add a `[bans].multiple-versions = "allow"` exception for `tokio` and `async-trait` (so legitimate bumps don't trip the lint).[m
[32m+[m[32m- Document the fleet convention in a comment at the top of each `deny.toml`: "pheno-* convention: tokio is the sole async runtime. async-std / smol / futures-runtime are forbidden."[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### R-6 (P3 / MSRV): Document and align the Rust MSRV floor[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m`pheno-port-adapter/Cargo.toml:5` declares `rust-version = "1.82"`. `pheno-tracing/Cargo.toml:5` and `pheno-otel/Cargo.toml:5` declare `rust-version = "1.75"`. `pheno-errors/Cargo.toml` and `pheno-config/Cargo.toml` declare no MSRV at all.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Action:**[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m- Add `rust-version = "1.82"` to `pheno-errors/Cargo.toml` and verify it builds.[m
[32m+[m[32m- Decide whether the fleet floor should be 1.75 (lower barrier) or 1.82 (matches the highest individual crate). Document the choice in the new ADR-088.[m
[32m+[m[32m- If 1.82 is the floor, verify no other pheno-* crate pins `< 1.82`.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m## 7. Decision Matrix — Accept / Modify / Defer[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m| Rec | Effort | Value | Recommendation |[m
[32m+[m[32m|---|---|---|---|[m
[32m+[m[32m| R-1 (minimal tokio features) | 1h | M | **ACCEPT** — trim `pheno-tracing`'s `"full"` to the canonical set; add CI lint |[m
[32m+[m[32m| R-2 (unify dev-deps tokio features) | 15m | M | **ACCEPT** — one-line patch in `pheno-port-adapter/Cargo.toml:34` |[m
[32m+[m[32m| R-3 (sparse-checkout fix for pheno-config) | 5m | L | **ACCEPT** — update `.git/info/sparse-checkout` cone |[m
[32m+[m[32m| R-4 (author ADR-088 doc) | 1h | M | **ACCEPT** — write `docs/architecture/async-runtime-decision.md` |[m
[32m+[m[32m| R-5 (deny.toml ban on competing runtimes) | 30m | L | **ACCEPT** — convention-enforcement, low-cost |[m
[32m+[m[32m| R-6 (align MSRV floor) | 30m | M | **ACCEPT** — pick 1.82, update 3 Cargo.toml files |[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Combined effort:** ~3.5h wall, ~150 LoC across 5-7 files. All P3 (informational / nice-to-have). No P0/P1/P2 blockers found.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m## 8. Working-Tree Volatility Note[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mDuring the audit window (2026-06-21 13:30-13:50 PDT), the monorepo's working tree changed in ways that affected this audit:[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m- `pheno-context/` was present with `src/oidc.rs` at audit start, and contained tokio usage (`use tokio::sync::RwLock`, `#[tokio::test]`, `async fn`). By audit end, the directory was empty at the root; the v19 T3 OIDC federation track work landed and replaced the async implementation with a synchronous `parking_lot::RwLock`-based version in `FocalPoint/pheno-context/src/oidc.rs`. The earlier draft of this finding used `pheno-context` as the 5th repo; the final draft uses `pheno-config` for verifiability.[m
[32m+[m[32m- `pheno-config/` gained a `Cargo.lock` mid-audit (was absent at start; present at end). The lock shows only `zeroize 1.9.0` as a non-pheno-config dep — confirming sync-only.[m
[32m+[m[32m- No `pheno-errors`, `pheno-otel`, `pheno-port-adapter`, or `pheno-tracing` files were modified during the audit window. Their data is stable.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mIf this audit needs to be re-run, prefer a clean checkout (no in-flight v19 T3 work) for stable citations.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m## 9. Closure[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mSIDE-10 is **complete**. The fleet passes the v17 T6 / L10 consistency gate by adoption: 100 % tokio, no fragmentation, lock-resolved versions identical where verifiable.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mThe recommendations in § 6 are all P3 polish; none gate v19 cycle-9 P1 work. They are eligible for a single follow-up sweep, e.g. "SIDE-10 follow-up: tokio feature-flag standardization + ADR-088 authoring" in v20 planning.[m
