[32m+[m[32m# v19 — 71-Pillar Cycle 9 (P1 Reduction Wave)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Date:** 2026-06-21 19:30 PDT (v18 closed 2026-06-21 18:45 PDT — 47/47 P0 pillars, fleet mean 2.86)[m
[32m+[m[32m**Status:** ACTIVE[m
[32m+[m[32m**Supersedes:** v18 cycle 8 (P0 closure wave)[m
[32m+[m[32m**Target:** Drive 4-6 P1 pillars → SOTA score (3) where they currently sit at 1.5-2.0[m
[32m+[m[32m**Architecture:** 5 tracks × parallel (mostly macbook-safe, no cargo contention risk)[m
[32m+[m[32m**Critical path:** ~3 weeks wall-clock, ~5 PRs, ~1,500 LOC[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m## 1. Executive Summary[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mv18 closed **all 47 P0 pillars** (Architecture, Performance, Quality, DX, UX, Security, Observability, Documentation, Governance). The fleet mean hit **2.86** (target met). What remains:[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m- **15 pillars at 2.0** (Adequate) — these are the P1 targets. Each has a clear upgrade path.[m
[32m+[m[32m- **5 pillars at 1.5** (Minimal) — the hardest gaps, mostly in performance benchmarking (L19) and encryption enforcement (L52).[m
[32m+[m[32m- **27 pillars at 2.5** (Solid) — gradual improvements only.[m
[32m+[m[32m- **0 pillars at 3.0** (SOTA) — out of scope for v19; reserved for v20+ cycle.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mv19 is the **P1 reduction wave**. Goal: move 4-6 pillars from "Adequate" to "Solid" by closing the documentation + tooling gaps surfaced in v18 cycle 8 probe §6.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m## 2. Scope (the 5 tracks)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### Track T1 — L50 Vault Implementation Plan (the headline)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Owner:** orchestrator + subagent on heavy-runner[m
[32m+[m[32m**Wall-clock:** ~1 week[m
[32m+[m[32m**LOC:** ~600 (docs + scripts; no actual Vault deployment)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mPer v18 probe §6 finding 1, the **L50 Secrets Management** pillar scored 1.5 because no concrete plan exists for migrating from `.env` + GitHub Secrets to HashiCorp Vault + OIDC dynamic credentials.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Deliverables:**[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m1. `docs/adr/2026-06-21/ADR-077-vault-migration-roadmap.md` (350 LOC)[m
[32m+[m[32m   - 4-phase plan: (1) Vault dev cluster, (2) OIDC integration, (3) workflow migration, (4) full rollout[m
[32m+[m[32m   - 12-week timeline + 3 team-FTE budget[m
[32m+[m[32m   - ADR-046 (federation mTLS+OIDC) compatibility[m
[32m+[m[32m   - Risk register (5 items) + mitigation[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m2. `docs/architecture/secrets-management-convention.md` (200 LOC)[m
[32m+[m[32m   - Vault path conventions (`secret/data/pheno/{env}/{app}/{role}`)[m
[32m+[m[32m   - OIDC binding for CI (GitHub Actions, Buildkite, Jenkins)[m
[32m+[m[32m   - Dynamic credential rotation (15min TTL for AWS, 24h for database)[m
[32m+[m[32m   - Migration runbook from `.env`[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m3. `scripts/vault_smoke.sh` (50 LOC)[m
[32m+[m[32m   - Bash + curl + jq: POST to Vault dev server, retrieve + decrypt a test secret, assert rotation works[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Score target:** L50 1.5 → 2.0 (Adequate)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### Track T2 — L52 Encryption-at-Rest Mandate[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Owner:** orchestrator[m
[32m+[m[32m**Wall-clock:** ~3 days[m
[32m+[m[32m**LOC:** ~300 (mostly docs + 1 CI check)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mPer v18 probe §6 finding 2, **L52 (Encryption-at-Rest)** sits at 1.5 because no fleet-wide policy exists. Substrate crates (pheno-config, pheno-port-adapter) handle secrets in plaintext in memory, no `zeroize` enforcement.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Deliverables:**[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m1. `docs/adr/2026-06-21/ADR-078-encryption-at-rest-mandate.md` (200 LOC)[m
[32m+[m[32m   - Policy: ALL secret material (API keys, tokens, passwords) MUST use `zeroize::Zeroize` on Drop[m
[32m+[m[32m   - Cargo deny rule: ban `String::from_utf8(secret_bytes)` + similar unsafe patterns[m
[32m+[m[32m   - Devcontainer + Dockerfile: encrypt swap + tmpfs[m
[32m+[m[32m   - AWS: enforce EBS encryption + S3 default encryption (terraform module reference)[m
[32m+[m[32m   - Kubernetes: enforce encryption at rest on PersistentVolumes (NetworkPolicy + StorageClass)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m2. `.cargo/audit-rules.toml` (50 LOC) — `cargo-deny` config: deny `unsafe_code` in secret-handling modules (pheno-config, pheno-port-adapter)[m
[32m+[m[32m3. `pheno-config/src/secrets.rs` — add `#[derive(ZeroizeOnDrop)]` to all 3 secret-holding structs (~50 LOC)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Score target:** L52 1.5 → 2.0[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### Track T3 — L54 OIDC for Service-to-Service[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Owner:** orchestrator + subagent on heavy-runner[m
[32m+[m[32m**Wall-clock:** ~5 days[m
[32m+[m[32m**LOC:** ~500 (spec + reference implementation)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mPer v18 probe §6 finding 3, **L54 (Federated Identity)** scored 2.0 because ADR-046 exists but no concrete OIDC implementation. This track produces the **reference OIDC client** for federated service-to-service auth.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Deliverables:**[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m1. `docs/adr/2026-06-21/ADR-079-oidc-federation-reference.md` (250 LOC)[m
[32m+[m[32m   - 3 OIDC providers supported: Auth0, Okta, Keycloak[m
[32m+[m[32m   - JWKS caching + key rotation[m
[32m+[m[32m   - Token claim → PhenoContext mapping[m
[32m+[m[32m   - Failure modes (network partition, provider down, expired token)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m2. `pheno-context/src/oidc.rs` (200 LOC) — `OidcClient` struct with `verify_id_token()`, `refresh()`, `userinfo()` methods + 3 unit tests[m
[32m+[m[32m3. `examples/oidc_consumer/` (50 LOC) — example web service that consumes the OIDC bearer token + links to Auth0/Keycloak sandbox[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Score target:** L54 2.0 → 2.5[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### Track T4 — L19 Performance Benchmarking Infrastructure (deepening)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Owner:** subagent on heavy-runner (macbook unsafe — >10min cargo builds)[m
[32m+[m[32m**Wall-clock:** ~2 days[m
[32m+[m[32m**LOC:** ~200 (benchmarks + harness)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mPer v18 probe §6 finding 4, **L19 (Performance Benchmarks)** sits at 2.0 — we have criterion benches for 1-2 crates but no fleet-wide harness. This track adds **fleet-wide perf gates** in CI.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Deliverables:**[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m1. `benchmarks/fleet-perf.toml` (100 LOC) — declarative manifest of all perf benchmarks (pheno-config, pheno-port-adapter, pheno-flags, pheno-mcp-router, phenotype-dep-guard) with budget per method (e.g., `parse_cargo: p95 < 50ms`)[m
[32m+[m[32m2. `scripts/perf_gate.py` (50 LOC) — runs all benchmarks in sequence, asserts each budget, returns 0/1[m
[32m+[m[32m3. `.github/workflows/perf-gate.yml` (50 LOC) — nightly + on-PR workflow that runs `perf_gate.py` and posts results to findings/[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Score target:** L19 2.0 → 2.5[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### Track T5 — L53 Bug Bounty + Pen Test Roadmap[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Owner:** orchestrator[m
[32m+[m[32m**Wall-clock:** ~2 days[m
[32m+[m[32m**LOC:** ~150 (docs)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mPer v18 probe §6 finding 5, **L53 (Pen Testing)** scored 2.0 because no annual cadence exists. This track writes the **roadmap**.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Deliverables:**[m
[32m+[m

[32m+[m[32m   - Annual cadence: 2× external pen tests (Q1 + Q3) + 1× bug bounty (Q2)[m
[32m+[m[32m   - Scope: all 47 active repos, all 9 substrate crates[m
[32m+[m[32m   - Vendor shortlist: Trail of Bits, Cure53, HackerOne, Bugcrowd[m
[32m+[m[32m   - Budget: $45K/year (pen test) + $20K/year (bounty min) + $100K max payout[m
[32m+[m[32m   - SLA: P0 24h, P1 7d, P2 30d[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Score target:** L53 2.0 → 2.5[m

[32m+[m[32m## 8. Success Metrics[m
[32m+[m

[32m+[m[32m## 2. Tracks (6 tracks)[m

[32m+[m[32m### Track T1 — L36 Chaos Engineering Depth (the headline)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Owner:** orchestrator + subagent on heavy-runner[m
[32m+[m[32m**Wall-clock:** ~1 week[m
[32m+[m[32m**LOC:** ~400 (new crate + adoption + CI)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mL11 (v17) introduced 5 ad-hoc `chaos_*.rs` test files. v20 ships the **reusable fault-injection framework** (`pheno-chaos` crate) that codifies the patterns: latency injection, fault scheduling, fault taxonomy (transient / permanent / cascading), automatic rollback on assertion failure.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Deliverables:**[m
[32m+[m[32m1. `crates/pheno-chaos/src/lib.rs` (250 LOC) — `FaultInjector`, `Fault`, `ChaosTest` traits + 5 built-in fault types[m
[32m+[m[32m2. `crates/pheno-chaos/tests/integration.rs` (100 LOC) — 8 integration tests[m
[32m+[m[32m3. Adopt in 3 substrate repos (pheno-port-adapter, pheno-mcp-router, pheno-config) with 1 chaos test each[m
[32m+[m[32m4. `.github/workflows/chaos-gate.yml` (50 LOC) — nightly chaos test run with fault-injection mandatory[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Score target:** L36 2.0 → 2.5[m

[32m+[m[32m- [ ] L1 reaches 3.0 (first fleet pillar at SOTA saturation)[m
[32m+[m[32m- [ ] L23, L27, L36, L44, L52 each reach 2.5 (5 pillars lifted ≥ +0.5)[m
[32m+[m[32m- [ ] Fleet mean reaches 2.95 → 3.02 (+0.07)[m
[32m+[m[32m- [ ] Architecture (AX) domain saturated at 3.00[m
[32m+[m[32m- [ ] 0 net content loss; 0 build breakages introduced[m
[32m+[m[32m- [ ] Cycle-10 probe documents the 3.00 breach as the **fleet-mean saturation milestone**[m
[32m+[m[32m- [ ] All work uses worklog v2.1 schema (per ADR-015 v2.1, ADR-025)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m## 7. Open Questions[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m1. **L36 domain classification:** The v19 cycle 9 probe §6 lists L36 as "Quality" but the L-numbering in `docs/adr/2026-06-17/ADR-024-71-pillar-audit-framework.md` places L36 in the DX range (L28-L37). The probe's classification appears to be a labeling slip. Resolution: treat L36 as DX L36 (Developer Experience: fault-injection framework) for v20 scoring purposes. **Owner: orchestrator at v20 kickoff.**[m
[32m+[m[32m2. **T6 L1 ADR-index toolchain:** Python or Rust for the generator script? Python is faster to write but Rust is consistent with the fleet substrate. Resolution: Python for the v20 generator (1-week timeline); Rust port in v21+ if the index becomes a critical-path tool.[m
[32m+[m[32m3. **T4 L44 deep-dive subject crates:** Are pheno-config + pheno-port-adapter + pheno-mcp-router the right 3? Or should it be the 3 hottest crates per L19 perf-gate findings? Resolution: defer to T4 subagent to pick the 3 with the highest p95 absolute time (not the highest delta).[m
[32m+[m[32m4. **T5 L52 cherry-pick safety:** The `chore/bootstrap-meta-bundle-2026-06-21` branch is on `pheno-config`. Will `git cherry-pick` from there to `pheno-config:main` conflict? Resolution: subagent verifies with `git merge-tree` before commit; if conflict, fall back to a fresh port from ADR-078 spec.[m
[32m+[m[32m5. **Fleet-mean breach implications:** Crossing 3.00 means the fleet is technically "above saturation." Should the v21+ scoring cap at 3.00 (as N/A treatment already does) or allow 3.01-3.05? Resolution: keep raw arithmetic mean; document the breach in the cycle-10 probe.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m---[m

[32m+[m[32m## 3. Track specifications[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### T1 — L1 Architecture ADR consolidation (2.5 → 3.0)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Goal:** Consolidate the 47 ADRs across 7 dates into a single cross-referenced index with auto-generated backlinks.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Deliverables:**[m
[32m+[m[32m1. `docs/adr/INDEX.md` — single canonical entry point with 47 ADR rows + status + scope[m
[32m+[m[32m2. `scripts/adr_index_gen.py` — auto-gen script (parses ADR files, builds index)[m
[32m+[m[32m3. `scripts/adr_backlink_check.py` — verifies every ADR cross-ref points to a real file[m
[32m+[m[32m4. CI gate: `.github/workflows/adr-lint.yml` — fails PR if backlinks are stale[m
[32m+[m[32m5. ADR docstring lint: each ADR must have a "## Cross-references" section[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Acceptance:** `adr_index_gen.py` produces 47-row table; `adr_backlink_check.py` exits 0; CI workflow triggers on ADR changes.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### T2 — L44 Performance flamegraph deep-dives (2.0 → 2.5)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Goal:** Add flamegraph-driven optimization loop for 3 fleet-critical crates (config, tracing, mcp-router).[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Deliverables:**[m
[32m+[m[32m1. `benchmarks/flamegraph/` — `cargo-flamegraph` integration + scripts[m
[32m+[m[32m2. `benchmarks/flamegraph/config-baseline.svg` — baseline flamegraph for pheno-config[m
[32m+[m[32m3. `benchmarks/flamegraph/tracing-baseline.svg` — baseline flamegraph for pheno-tracing[m
[32m+[m[32m4. `benchmarks/flamegraph/mcp-router-baseline.svg` — baseline flamegraph for pheno-mcp-router[m
[32m+[m[32m5. `findings/2026-06-22-v20-T2-L44-flamegraph-deep-dives.md` — analysis report[m
[32m+[m[32m6. Optimization opportunities logged in `findings/2026-06-22-v20-T2-L44-opportunities.md`[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Acceptance:** 3 flamegraph SVGs checked in; opportunities doc identifies ≥ 5 actionable optimizations.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### T3 — L36 Chaos fault-injection framework (2.0 → 2.5)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Goal:** Build a reusable fault-injection primitive and adopt it in 3 crates (network, fs, async-runtime).[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Deliverables:**[m
[32m+[m[32m1. `chaos-injection/` (new substrate primitive crate) — `Fault` enum + injection points[m
[32m+[m[32m2. `chaos-injection/src/lib.rs` — public API[m
[32m+[m[32m3. `chaos-injection/src/inject.rs` — fault injection at runtime[m
[32m+[m[32m4. Adoption tests in 3 crates: `pheno-fs`, `pheno-net`, `pheno-async`[m
[32m+[m[32m5. `findings/2026-06-22-v20-T3-L36-fault-injection-framework.md`[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Acceptance:** `chaos-injection` builds clean; 3 adoption tests pass; framework is reusable.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### T4 — L27 Pact consumer-driven contract tests (2.0 → 2.5)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Goal:** Add Pact contract tests across 2 federated services (mcp-router ↔ tracing, mcp-router ↔ events).[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Deliverables:**[m
[32m+[m[32m1. `pact-consumer/` (new test fixture crate) — Pact broker setup + provider stubs[m
[32m+[m[32m2. Consumer contract: `pheno-mcp-router/pact/contracts/mcp-tracing.json`[m
[32m+[m[32m3. Consumer contract: `pheno-mcp-router/pact/contracts/mcp-events.json`[m
[32m+[m[32m4. Provider verification: 2 test files in `pheno-tracing/pact/` + `pheno-events/pact/`[m
[32m+[m[32m5. `findings/2026-06-22-v20-T4-L27-pact-contract-tests.md`[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Acceptance:** 2 consumer contracts published; 2 provider verifications pass; can-i-deploy check works.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### T5 — L23 `proptest::Arbitrary` impls (2.0 → 2.5)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Goal:** Add `Arbitrary` derive to 8 of 11 substrate crates so proptest can fuzz them automatically.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Deliverables:**[m
[32m+[m[32m1. `proptest` derive added to 8 crates: pheno-config, pheno-context, pheno-errors, pheno-flags, pheno-port-adapter, pheno-otel, pheno-tracing, pheno-events[m
[32m+[m[32m2. Property tests: 1 new test per crate (10 lines each, exercises random valid inputs)[m
[32m+[m[32m3. CI integration: `.github/workflows/proptest.yml` runs all 8 new tests nightly[m
[32m+[m[32m4. `findings/2026-06-22-v20-T5-L23-proptest-arbitrary.md`[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m**Acceptance:** 8 crates have `Arbitrary` impls; 8 new property tests pass; CI workflow runs.[m

[1m+++ b/scripts/adr_backlink_check.py[m
[36m@@ -0,0 +1,164 @@[m
[32m+[m[32m#!/usr/bin/env python3[m
[32m+[m[32m"""Verify ADR cross-references resolve to existing ADRs.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mFor each ADR in the index, this script parses the body for cross-reference[m
[32m+[m[32msections (`## See Also`, `## References`, `## Related`, `## Related Decisions`),[m
[32m+[m[32mextracts ADR-### and ADR-###B mentions, and verifies each one points to an[m
[32m+[m[32mexisting ADR file.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mExit codes:[m
[32m+[m[32m  0  all references resolve[m
[32m+[m[32m  1  one or more unresolved references (broken cross-references)[m
[32m+[m[32m  2  internal error[m
[32m+[m[32m  3  bad CLI args[m
[32m+[m[32m  130 keyboard interrupt[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mIdempotent and fast: walks ADR files once, no network calls, no git ops.[m
[32m+[m[32m"""[m
[32m+[m[32mfrom __future__ import annotations[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mimport argparse[m
[32m+[m[32mimport re[m
[32m+[m[32mimport sys[m
[32m+[m[32mfrom collections import defaultdict[m
[32m+[m[32mfrom pathlib import Path[m
[32m+[m[32mfrom typing import Iterable, NamedTuple[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mREPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent[m
[32m+[m[32mADR_ROOT = REPO_ROOT / "docs" / "adr"[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mCROSSREF_SECTION_RE = re.compile([m
[32m+[m[32m    r"^(#{2,3})\s+(?:See Also|References|Related(?:\s+Decisions)?|Cross[ -]References?)\s*$",[m
[32m+[m[32m    re.MULTILINE | re.IGNORECASE,[m
[32m+[m[32m)[m
[32m+[m[32mNEXT_HEADING_RE = re.compile(r"^(#{1,3})\s+.+$", re.MULTILINE)[m
[32m+[m[32mADR_REF_RE = re.compile(r"\bADR-(\d+)(B?)\b", re.IGNORECASE)[m
[32m+[m[32mADR_FILENAME_RE = re.compile(r"^ADR-(\d+)(B?)-.+\.md$", re.IGNORECASE)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mclass BrokenRef(NamedTuple):[m
[32m+[m[32m    adr_id: str[m
[32m+[m[32m    missing_ref: str[m
[32m+[m[32m    section: str[m
[32m+[m[32m    line: int[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mdef list_adr_files() -> list[Path]:[m
[32m+[m[32m    if not ADR_ROOT.exists():[m
[32m+[m[32m        return [][m
[32m+[m[32m    out: list[Path] = [][m
[32m+[m[32m    for path in sorted(ADR_ROOT.rglob("ADR-*.md")):[m
[32m+[m[32m        if path.name.upper() == "INDEX.MD":[m
[32m+[m[32m            continue[m
[32m+[m[32m        if ADR_FILENAME_RE.match(path.name):[m
[32m+[m[32m            out.append(path)[m
[32m+[m[32m    return out[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mdef extract_crossref_sections(body: str) -> Iterable[tuple[str, str, int]]:[m
[32m+[m[32m    for match in CROSSREF_SECTION_RE.finditer(body):[m
[32m+[m[32m        start = match.start()[m
[32m+[m[32m        heading_text = match.group(0).lstrip("#").strip()[m
[32m+[m[32m        start_line = body.count("\n", 0, start) + 1[m
[32m+[m[32m        current_level = len(match.group(1))[m
[32m+[m[32m        end = len(body)[m
[32m+[m[32m        for nxt in NEXT_HEADING_RE.finditer(body, start + len(match.group(0))):[m
[32m+[m[32m            if len(nxt.group(1)) <= current_level:[m
[32m+[m[32m                end = nxt.start()[m
[32m+[m[32m                break[m
[32m+[m[32m        section_text = body[start:end][m
[32m+[m[32m        yield (heading_text, section_text, start_line)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mdef references_in_section(section_text: str) -> list[str]:[m
[32m+[m[32m    refs = [][m
[32m+[m[32m    for m in ADR_REF_RE.finditer(section_text):[m
[32m+[m[32m        n, suffix = m.group(1), m.group(2)[m
[32m+[m[32m        refs.append(f"ADR-{int(n):03d}{suffix.upper()}")[m
[32m+[m[32m    return refs[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mdef check_file(path: Path, known_adr_ids: set[str]) -> list[BrokenRef]:[m
[32m+[m[32m    body = path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")[m
[32m+[m[32m    adr_id_match = ADR_FILENAME_RE.match(path.name)[m
[32m+[m[32m    if not adr_id_match:[m
[32m+[m[32m        return [][m
[32m+[m[32m    n, suffix = adr_id_match.group(1), adr_id_match.group(2)[m
[32m+[m[32m    this_id = f"ADR-{int(n):03d}{suffix.upper()}"[m
[32m+[m[32m    broken: list[BrokenRef] = [][m
[32m+[m[32m    for section_name, section_text, line_no in extract_crossref_sections(body):[m
[32m+[m[32m        for ref in references_in_section(section_text):[m
[32m+[m[32m            if ref == this_id:[m
[32m+[m[32m                continue[m
[32m+[m[32m            if ref not in known_adr_ids:[m
[32m+[m[32m                broken.append(BrokenRef(this_id, ref, section_name, line_no))[m
[32m+[m[32m    return broken[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mdef main() -> int:[m
[32m+[m[32m    p = argparse.ArgumentParser([m
[32m+[m[32m        description="Verify ADR cross-references resolve to existing ADRs."[m
[32m+[m[32m    )[m
[32m+[m[32m    p.add_argument("--strict", action="store_true",[m
[32m+[m[32m                   help="Fail if any ADR has no cross-reference section at all.")[m
[32m+[m[32m    p.add_argument("--quiet", action="store_true",[m
[32m+[m[32m                   help="Only print errors (no success summary).")[m
[32m+[m[32m    args = p.parse_args()[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    files = list_adr_files()[m
[32m+[m[32m    known_ids = set()[m
[32m+[m[32m    for f in files:[m
[32m+[m[32m        m = ADR_FILENAME_RE.match(f.name)[m
[32m+[m[32m        if m:[m
[32m+[m[32m            n, s = m.group(1), m.group(2)[m
[32m+[m[32m            known_ids.add(f"ADR-{int(n):03d}{s.upper()}")[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    if not args.quiet:[m
[32m+[m[32m        print(f"Found {len(files)} ADR files; {len(known_ids)} unique identifiers.")[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    by_source: dict[str, list[BrokenRef]] = defaultdict(list)[m
[32m+[m[32m    no_sections: list[str] = [][m
[32m+[m[32m    for f in files:[m
[32m+[m[32m        m = ADR_FILENAME_RE.match(f.name)[m
[32m+[m[32m        if not m:[m
[32m+[m[32m            continue[m
[32m+[m[32m        this_id = f"ADR-{int(m.group(1)):03d}{m.group(2).upper()}"[m
[32m+[m[32m        broken = check_file(f, known_ids)[m
[32m+[m[32m        by_source[this_id].extend(broken)[m
[32m+[m[32m        body = f.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")[m
[32m+[m[32m        sections = list(extract_crossref_sections(body))[m
[32m+[m[32m        if not sections and args.strict:[m
[32m+[m[32m            no_sections.append(this_id)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    total_broken = sum(len(v) for v in by_source.values())[m
[32m+[m[32m    if total_broken == 0 and not no_sections:[m
[32m+[m[32m        if not args.quiet:[m
[32m+[m[32m            print("OK: all ADR cross-references resolve.")[m
[32m+[m[32m        return 0[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    if total_broken > 0:[m
[32m+[m[32m        print(f"\nFAIL: {total_broken} broken cross-reference(s):", file=sys.stderr)[m
[32m+[m[32m        for source_id in sorted(by_source):[m
[32m+[m[32m            for ref in by_source[source_id]:[m
[32m+[m[32m                print([m
[32m+[m[32m                    f"  {source_id} ({ref.section}, L{ref.line}): "[m
[32m+[m[32m                    f"-> {ref.missing_ref} (not found in repo)",[m
[32m+[m[32m                    file=sys.stderr,[m
[32m+[m[32m                )[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    if no_sections:[m
[32m+[m[32m        print([m
[32m+[m[32m            f"\nWARN: {len(no_sections)} ADR(s) have no cross-reference section:",[m
[32m+[m[32m            file=sys.stderr,[m
[32m+[m[32m        )[m
[32m+[m[32m        for adr_id in sorted(no_sections):[m
[32m+[m[32m            print(f"  {adr_id}", file=sys.stderr)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    return 1 if total_broken > 0 else 0[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mif __name__ == "__main__":[m
[32m+[m[32m    try:[m
[32m+[m[32m        sys.exit(main())[m
[32m+[m[32m    except KeyboardInterrupt:[m
[32m+[m[32m        sys.exit(130)[m

[1mnew file mode 100644[m
[1mindex 0000000000..859b5e8188[m
[1m--- /dev/null[m
[1m+++ b/scripts/adr_index_gen.py[m
[36m@@ -0,0 +1,172 @@[m
[32m+[m[32m#!/usr/bin/env python3[m
[32m+[m[32m"""[m
[32m+[m[32madr_index_gen.py - Regenerate docs/adr/INDEX.md (chronological table).[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mScans docs/adr/**/*.md for ADR files, extracts ADR number, title, status,[m
[32m+[m[32mdate, scope summary, and supersedes-link from each, and writes a single[m
[32m+[m[32mchronological Markdown table to docs/adr/INDEX.md.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mStatus values are normalized to one of: PROPOSED, ACCEPTED, SUPERSEDED,[m
[32m+[m[32mACCEPTED (CLOSED), or the raw value if unrecognized. The pillar-grouped[m
[32m+[m[32mview (hand-curated) lives at docs/adr/INDEX-by-pillar.md; this script[m
[32m+[m[32mwrites only the chronological table.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mUsage:[m
[32m+[m[32m    python3 scripts/adr_index_gen.py [--root PATH] [--out PATH][m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mExit 0 on success, 2 on I/O error.[m
[32m+[m[32m"""[m
[32m+[m[32mimport argparse[m
[32m+[m[32mimport re[m
[32m+[m[32mimport sys[m
[32m+[m[32mfrom datetime import datetime, timezone[m
[32m+[m[32mfrom pathlib import Path[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mADR_NUM_RE = re.compile(r"ADR-(\d{3})")[m
[32m+[m[32mH1_RE = re.compile(r"^#\s+ADR-\d+[^\n]*", re.MULTILINE)[m
[32m+[m[32mSTATUS_RE = re.compile([m
[32m+[m[32m    r"\*\*\s*Status\*\*?\s*[:|]\s*\*?\*?([A-Za-z][A-Za-z0-9 ()/—\-]*)", re.MULTILINE[m
[32m+[m[32m)[m
[32m+[m[32mDATE_RE = re.compile(r"\*\*\s*Date\*\*?\s*[:|]\s*\*?\*?(\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2})", re.MULTILINE)[m
[32m+[m[32mSUPERSEDES_RE = re.compile(r"\*\*\s*Supersedes\*\*?\s*[:|]\s*([^\n]+)")[m
[32m+[m[32mSUMMARY_RE = re.compile(r"^##\s+Context\s*\n+([^\n#][^\n]*)", re.MULTILINE)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mdef parse_adr(path: Path):[m
[32m+[m[32m    """Return dict for one ADR file, or None if filename is not an ADR."""[m
[32m+[m[32m    m = ADR_NUM_RE.search(path.name)[m
[32m+[m[32m    if not m:[m
[32m+[m[32m        return None[m
[32m+[m[32m    num = int(m.group(1))[m
[32m+[m[32m    text = path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    h1 = H1_RE.search(text)[m
[32m+[m[32m    title = h1.group(0).lstrip("# ").strip() if h1 else path.stem[m
[32m+[m[32m    title = re.sub(r"^ADR-\d+[\s:—\-]+", "", title).strip()[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    status = STATUS_RE.search(text)[m
[32m+[m[32m    status_raw = status.group(1).strip() if status else "UNKNOWN"[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    date = DATE_RE.search(text)[m
[32m+[m[32m    date_str = date.group(1) if date else ""[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    sup = SUPERSEDES_RE.search(text)[m
[32m+[m[32m    sup_str = sup.group(1).strip() if sup else ""[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    sm = SUMMARY_RE.search(text)[m
[32m+[m[32m    summary = " ".join(sm.group(1).split())[:240] if sm else ""[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    return {[m
[32m+[m[32m        "num": num,[m
[32m+[m[32m        "title": title,[m
[32m+[m[32m        "status": status_raw,[m
[32m+[m[32m        "date": date_str,[m
[32m+[m[32m        "summary": summary,[m
[32m+[m[32m        "supersedes": sup_str,[m
[32m+[m[32m        "rel_path": str(path),[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mdef normalize_status(s: str) -> str:[m
[32m+[m[32m    """Map raw status text to a canonical display value."""[m
[32m+[m[32m    u = s.upper()[m
[32m+[m[32m    if "SUPERSEDED" in u:[m
[32m+[m[32m        return "SUPERSEDED"[m
[32m+[m[32m    if "PROPOSED" in u:[m
[32m+[m[32m        return "PROPOSED"[m
[32m+[m[32m    if "ACCEPTED" in u or "CLOSED" in u:[m
[32m+[m[32m        return "ACCEPTED" if "CLOSED" not in u else "ACCEPTED (CLOSED)"[m
[32m+[m[32m    return s[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mdef render_table(rows, root):[m
[32m+[m[32m    """Return the full chronological INDEX.md body as a single string."""[m
[32m+[m[32m    now = datetime.now(timezone.utc).strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M UTC")[m
[32m+[m[32m    lines = [[m
[32m+[m[32m        "# ADR Index - Chronological Cross-Reference",[m
[32m+[m[32m        "",[m
[32m+[m[32m        f"**Generated:** {now}  ",[m
[32m+[m[32m        f"**Source:** {len(rows)} ADR file(s) under `{root}/`  ",[m
[32m+[m[32m        "**Generator:** `scripts/adr_index_gen.py` (v20 T1)  ",[m
[32m+[m[32m        "**Pillar-grouped view:** `docs/adr/INDEX-by-pillar.md` (hand-curated)  ",[m
[32m+[m[32m        "**Backlink validator:** `scripts/adr_backlink_check.py`  ",[m
[32m+[m[32m        "",[m
[32m+[m[32m        "## Master Table",[m
[32m+[m[32m        "",[m
[32m+[m[32m        "| # | ADR | Date | Status | Title | Scope summary | Supersedes |",[m
[32m+[m[32m        "|---:|-----|------|--------|-------|---------------|------------|",[m
[32m+[m[32m    ][m
[32m+[m[32m    for r in rows:[m
[32m+[m[32m        s = normalize_status(r["status"])[m
[32m+[m[32m        summary = r["summary"].replace("|", "\\|")[m
[32m+[m[32m        sup = r["supersedes"].replace("|", "\\|") or "-"[m
[32m+[m[32m        title = r["title"][:80].replace("|", "\\|")[m
[32m+[m[32m        lines.append([m
[32m+[m[32m            f"| {r['num']:03d} | "[m
[32m+[m[32m            f"[{r['num']:03d}]({r['rel_path']}) | "[m
[32m+[m[32m            f"{r['date']} | {s} | {title} | "[m
[32m+[m[32m            f"{summary[:200]} | {sup[:60]} |"[m
[32m+[m[32m        )[m
[32m+[m[32m    lines.extend([[m
[32m+[m[32m        "",[m
[32m+[m[32m        "---",[m
[32m+[m[32m        "",[m
[32m+[m[32m        "## Notes",[m
[32m+[m[32m        "",[m
[32m+[m[32m        "- This file is **auto-generated** by `scripts/adr_index_gen.py`. "[m
[32m+[m[32m        "Do not edit by hand; the `adr-lint` CI workflow fails if it "[m
[32m+[m[32m        "drifts from the on-disk ADRs.",[m
[32m+[m[32m        "- The hand-curated **pillar-grouped** view lives at "[m
[32m+[m[32m        "`docs/adr/INDEX-by-pillar.md` (per ADR-024 + ADR-041; cadence: "[m
[32m+[m[32m        "weekly Mon 09:00 PDT).",[m
[32m+[m[32m        "- ADR numbers may collide across date directories (e.g. ADR-077 "[m
[32m+[m[32m        "in `2026-06-20/` is SLSA, ADR-077 in `2026-06-21/` is Vault). "[m
[32m+[m[32m        "Disambiguation is by file path.",[m
[32m+[m[32m        "- Cross-references in ADR bodies are validated by "[m
[32m+[m[32m        "`scripts/adr_backlink_check.py` (run on every ADR-touching PR).",[m
[32m+[m[32m        "",[m
[32m+[m[32m        f"<!-- generated: {now} by scripts/adr_index_gen.py -->",[m
[32m+[m[32m    ])[m
[32m+[m[32m    return "\n".join(lines)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mdef main():[m
[32m+[m[32m    p = argparse.ArgumentParser(description=__doc__.splitlines()[0])[m
[32m+[m[32m    p.add_argument("--root", default="docs/adr", help="ADR root directory")[m
[32m+[m[32m    p.add_argument("--out", default="docs/adr/INDEX.md", help="Output path")[m
[32m+[m[32m    p.add_argument([m
[32m+[m[32m        "--check",[m
[32m+[m[32m        action="store_true",[m
[32m+[m[32m        help="Exit 1 if --out would change; do not write the file",[m
[32m+[m[32m    )[m
[32m+[m[32m    args = p.parse_args()[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    root = Path(args.root)[m
[32m+[m[32m    if not root.is_dir():[m
[32m+[m[32m        print(f"ERROR: ADR root {root} does not exist", file=sys.stderr)[m
[32m+[m[32m        return 2[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    files = sorted(root.rglob("ADR-*.md"))[m
[32m+[m[32m    rows = [r for r in (parse_adr(f) for f in files) if r is not None][m
[32m+[m[32m    rows.sort(key=lambda r: (r["num"], r["rel_path"]))[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    out = Path(args.out)[m
[32m+[m[32m    out.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    if args.check:[m
[32m+[m[32m        # Build the would-be table only and compare against existing file[m
[32m+[m[32m        new_text = render_table(rows, args.root)[m
[32m+[m[32m        existing = out.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace") if out.exists() else ""[m
[32m+[m[32m        if new_text != existing:[m
[32m+[m[32m            print(f"STALE: {out} would change ({len(rows)} ADR rows).", file=sys.stderr)[m
[32m+[m[32m            return 1[m
[32m+[m[32m        print(f"OK: {out} is fresh ({len(rows)} ADR rows).")[m
[32m+[m[32m        return 0[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    out.write_text(render_table(rows, args.root) + "\n", encoding="utf-8")[m
[32m+[m[32m    print(f"Wrote {out} ({len(rows)} rows)")[m
[32m+[m[32m    return 0[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mif __name__ == "__main__":[m
[32m+[m[32m    sys.exit(main())[m

[1m--- /dev/null[m

[32m+[m[32m#!/usr/bin/env bash[m
[32m+[m[32mset -euo pipefail[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mROOT="${1:-$(pwd)}"[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mcommit_repos=([m
[32m+[m[32m  Apisync AtomsBot-2nd AtomsBot-3rd AtomsBot-5th AuthKit bare-cua Civis[m
[32m+[m[32m  dinoforge-packs Eidolon eyetracker forgecode HexaKit KDesktopVirt MCPForge[m
[32m+[m[32m  nanovms OmniRoute-2nd Parpoura-5th PhenoDevOps PhenoProc phenotype-omlx[m
[32m+[m[32m  phenotype-ops-mcp portage ResilienceKit thegent-security-fixes[m
[32m+[m[32m)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mdiscard_repos=([m
[32m+[m[32m  agent-platform AgilePlus agslag-docs apps AtomsBot BytePort cheap-llm-mcp[m
[32m+[m[32m  Conft dispatch-mcp FocalPoint heliosBench HeliosCLI KaskMan KWatch-docs[m
[32m+[m[32m  localbase3 melosviz OmniRoute PhenoCompose PhenoHandbook PhenoKits[m
[32m+[m[32m  PhenoMCP-2nd PhenoProject PhenoRuntime PhenoSchema phenoShared[m
[32m+[m[32m  phenotype-dep-guard phenotype-hub phenotype-infra phenotype-journeys[m
[32m+[m[32m  phenotype-tooling PlayCua[m
[32m+[m[32m)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mstatus_clean() {[m
[32m+[m[32m  local repo="$1"[m
[32m+[m[32m  git -C "$ROOT/$repo" status --porcelain[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mcommit_repo() {[m
[32m+[m[32m  local repo="$1"[m
[32m+[m[32m  local message="${2:-chore: apply stash audit cleanup}"[m
[32m+[m[32m  if [[ -n "$(status_clean "$repo")" ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    git -C "$ROOT/$repo" add -A[m
[32m+[m[32m    git -C "$ROOT/$repo" commit -m "$message"[m
[32m+[m[32m  fi[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mdiscard_repo() {[m
[32m+[m[32m  local repo="$1"[m
[32m+[m[32m  if [[ -n "$(status_clean "$repo")" ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    git -C "$ROOT/$repo" stash push -u -m "l5-91 discard per STASH_AUDIT_2026_06_10 $repo" || true[m
[32m+[m[32m    git -C "$ROOT/$repo" stash drop 'stash@{0}' || true[m
[32m+[m[32m    git -C "$ROOT/$repo" restore --staged --worktree .[m
[32m+[m[32m    git -C "$ROOT/$repo" clean -ffdx[m
[32m+[m[32m  fi[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mfor repo in "${commit_repos[@]}"; do[m
[32m+[m[32m  commit_repo "$repo"[m
[32m+[m[32mdone[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mfor repo in "${discard_repos[@]}"; do[m
[32m+[m[32m  discard_repo "$repo"[m
[32m+[m[32mdone[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mgit -C "$ROOT/cheap-llm-mcp/.tmp-pr48-review" restore --staged --worktree . 2>/dev/null || true[m
[32m+[m[32mgit -C "$ROOT/cheap-llm-mcp/.tmp-pr48-review" clean -ffdx 2>/dev/null || true[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mif [[ -n "$(git -C "$ROOT/PhenoProc/Evalora" status --porcelain 2>/dev/null || true)" ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m  git -C "$ROOT/PhenoProc/Evalora" add -A[m
[32m+[m[32m  git -C "$ROOT/PhenoProc/Evalora" commit -m "chore: apply stash audit cleanup"[m
[32m+[m[32m  git -C "$ROOT/PhenoProc" add Evalora[m
[32m+[m[32m  git -C "$ROOT/PhenoProc" commit -m "chore: apply stash audit cleanup"[m
[32m+[m[32mfi[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mfailed=0[m
[32m+[m[32mfor repo in "${commit_repos[@]}" "${discard_repos[@]}"; do[m
[32m+[m[32m  if [[ -n "$(status_clean "$repo")" ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    echo "DIRTY $repo" >&2[m
[32m+[m[32m    failed=1[m
[32m+[m[32m  fi[m
[32m+[m[32mdone[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mexit "$failed"[m

[32m+[m[32m//! `perf_gate` binary — CLI entry point for the fleet performance gate.[m
[32m+[m[32m//![m
[32m+[m[32m//! Loads `benchmarks/fleet-perf.toml`, evaluates measured samples against each[m
[32m+[m[32m//! declared budget, prints a verdict in the requested format, and exits with[m
[32m+[m[32m//! a code reflecting the outcome.[m
[32m+[m[32m//![m
[32m+[m[32m//! Exit codes:[m
[32m+[m[32m//! - 0 — all budgets within ceiling (or only soft regressions when not[m
[32m+[m[32m//!       configured to fail on soft).[m
[32m+[m[32m//! - 1 — at least one hard regression.[m
[32m+[m[32m//! - 2 — soft regression present and `fail_on_soft_regression` is set.[m
[32m+[m[32m//![m
[32m+[m[32m//! Authority: ADR-040 + v19 71-pillar cycle 9 plan §2 Track T4.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32muse clap::Parser;[m
[32m+[m[32muse perf_gate::config::{GateConfig, OutputFormat};[m
[32m+[m[32muse perf_gate::gate::{Gate, GateVerdict, Regression, RegressionLevel};[m
[32m+[m[32muse perf_gate::report::{JsonReporter, MarkdownReporter, Reporter, TextReporter};[m
[32m+[m[32muse perf_gate::summary::fleet_summary;[m
[32m+[m[32muse std::path::PathBuf;[m
[32m+[m[32muse std::process::Command;[m
[32m+[m[32muse std::time::Instant;[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m#[derive(Parser, Debug)][m
[32m+[m[32m#[command([m
[32m+[m[32m    name = "perf_gate",[m
[32m+[m[32m    version,[m
[32m+[m[32m    about = "Fleet performance gate — evaluates fleet-perf.toml budgets"[m
[32m+[m[32m)][m
[32m+[m[32mstruct Cli {[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Path to the `fleet-perf.toml` manifest (overrides PERF_GATE_BUDGETS).[m
[32m+[m[32m    #[arg(long)][m
[32m+[m[32m    budgets: Option<PathBuf>,[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Treat soft-budget regressions as failures.[m
[32m+[m[32m    #[arg(long)][m
[32m+[m[32m    fail_on_soft_regression: bool,[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Output format: text (default), json, markdown.[m
[32m+[m[32m    #[arg(long, default_value = "text")][m
[32m+[m[32m    format: String,[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Skip actually running commands — measure zero samples (smoke test).[m
[32m+[m[32m    #[arg(long)][m
[32m+[m[32m    stub: bool,[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mfn main() {[m
[32m+[m[32m    let cli = Cli::parse();[m
[32m+[m[32m    // Build config: CLI flag > env var > default. from_env() does not[m
[32m+[m[32m    // validate the path; the explicit `validate()` call (or Gate::new's[m
[32m+[m[32m    // implicit budget read) surfaces a MissingBudgets error.[m
[32m+[m[32m    let mut config = match GateConfig::from_env() {[m
[32m+[m[32m        Ok(c) => c,[m
[32m+[m[32m        Err(e) => {[m
[32m+[m[32m            eprintln!("config error: {e}");[m
[32m+[m[32m            std::process::exit(2);[m
[32m+[m[32m        }[m
[32m+[m[32m    };[m
[32m+[m[32m    if let Some(p) = cli.budgets {[m
[32m+[m[32m        config.perf_budgets_path = p;[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m[32m    if cli.fail_on_soft_regression {[m
[32m+[m[32m        config.fail_on_soft_regression = true;[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m[32m    config.output_format = match cli.format.to_ascii_lowercase().as_str() {[m
[32m+[m[32m        "text" => OutputFormat::Text,[m
[32m+[m[32m        "json" => OutputFormat::Json,[m
[32m+[m[32m        "markdown" | "md" => OutputFormat::Markdown,[m
[32m+[m[32m        other => {[m
[32m+[m[32m            eprintln!("invalid --format value: {other}");[m
[32m+[m[32m            std::process::exit(2);[m
[32m+[m[32m        }[m
[32m+[m[32m    };[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    if let Err(e) = config.validate() {[m
[32m+[m[32m        eprintln!("config error: {e}");[m
[32m+[m[32m        std::process::exit(2);[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    let gate = match Gate::new(config.clone()) {[m
[32m+[m[32m        Ok(g) => g,[m
[32m+[m[32m        Err(e) => {[m
[32m+[m[32m            eprintln!("gate load error: {e}");[m
[32m+[m[32m            std::process::exit(2);[m
[32m+[m[32m        }[m
[32m+[m[32m    };[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    let verdicts = if cli.stub {[m
[32m+[m[32m        gate.budgets[m
[32m+[m[32m            .iter()[m
[32m+[m[32m            .map(|b| GateVerdict {[m
[32m+[m[32m                passed: true,[m
[32m+[m[32m                regressions: Vec::new(),[m
[32m+[m[32m                summary: format!("stub: skipped {}", b.name),[m
[32m+[m[32m            })[m
[32m+[m[32m            .collect::<Vec<_>>()[m
[32m+[m[32m    } else {[m
[32m+[m[32m        gate.budgets[m
[32m+[m[32m            .iter()[m
[32m+[m[32m            .map(|budget| evaluate_one(budget))[m
[32m+[m[32m            .collect()[m
[32m+[m[32m    };[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    let reporter: Box<dyn Reporter> = match config.output_format {[m
[32m+[m[32m        OutputFormat::Text => Box::new(TextReporter),[m
[32m+[m[32m        OutputFormat::Json => Box::new(JsonReporter),[m
[32m+[m[32m        OutputFormat::Markdown => Box::new(MarkdownReporter),[m
[32m+[m[32m    };[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    for v in &verdicts {[m
[32m+[m[32m        print!("{}", reporter.render(v));[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    println!("---\nFleet summary: {}", fleet_summary(&verdicts));[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    let any_hard = verdicts[m
[32m+[m[32m        .iter()[m
[32m+[m[32m        .flat_map(|v| v.regressions.iter())[m
[32m+[m[32m        .any(|r| matches!(r.level, RegressionLevel::Hard));[m
[32m+[m[32m    let any_soft = verdicts[m
[32m+[m[32m        .iter()[m
[32m+[m[32m        .flat_map(|v| v.regressions.iter())[m
[32m+[m[32m        .any(|r| matches!(r.level, RegressionLevel::Soft));[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    let exit_code = if any_hard {[m
[32m+[m[32m        1[m
[32m+[m[32m    } else if any_soft && config.fail_on_soft_regression {[m
[32m+[m[32m        2[m
[32m+[m[32m    } else {[m
[32m+[m[32m        0[m
[32m+[m[32m    };[m
[32m+[m[32m    std::process::exit(exit_code);[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mfn evaluate_one(budget: &perf_gate::budgets::PerformanceBudget) -> GateVerdict {[m
[32m+[m[32m    let mut samples = Vec::with_capacity(budget.runs as usize);[m
[32m+[m[32m    for _ in 0..budget.runs {[m
[32m+[m[32m        let t0 = Instant::now();[m
[32m+[m[32m        // The fleet-perf.toml uses `command = "true"` as a no-op stub. Real[m
[32m+[m[32m        // benchmarks will replace `command` with the crate's bench binary.[m
[32m+[m[32m        let _ = Command::new(&budget.command)[m
[32m+[m[32m            .args(&budget.args)[m
[32m+[m[32m            .output();[m
[32m+[m[32m        let elapsed_ms = t0.elapsed().as_secs_f64() * 1000.0;[m
[32m+[m[32m        samples.push(elapsed_ms);[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m[32m    let p95 = p95_of(&samples);[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    let mut regressions = Vec::new();[m
[32m+[m[32m    if matches!([m
[32m+[m[32m        budget.classify(p95),[m
[32m+[m[32m        perf_gate::budgets::BudgetClassification::Fail[m
[32m+[m[32m    ) {[m
[32m+[m[32m        let level = match budget.kind {[m
[32m+[m[32m            perf_gate::budgets::BudgetKind::Hard => RegressionLevel::Hard,[m
[32m+[m[32m            perf_gate::budgets::BudgetKind::Soft => RegressionLevel::Soft,[m
[32m+[m[32m        };[m
[32m+[m[32m        regressions.push(Regression {[m
[32m+[m[32m            budget_name: budget.name.clone(),[m
[32m+[m[32m            actual_ms: p95,[m
[32m+[m[32m            budget_ms: budget.p95_budget_ms as f64,[m
[32m+[m[32m            level,[m
[32m+[m[32m        });[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    let passed = regressions.is_empty();[m
[32m+[m[32m    let summary = if passed {[m
[32m+[m[32m        format!("{}: p95={:.3} ms within {} ms", budget.name, p95, budget.p95_budget_ms)[m
[32m+[m[32m    } else {[m
[32m+[m[32m        format!("{}: p95={:.3} ms EXCEEDS {} ms", budget.name, p95, budget.p95_budget_ms)[m
[32m+[m[32m    };[m
[32m+[m[32m    GateVerdict {[m
[32m+[m[32m        passed,[m
[32m+[m[32m        regressions,[m
[32m+[m[32m        summary,[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mfn p95_of(samples: &[f64]) -> f64 {[m
[32m+[m[32m    if samples.is_empty() {[m
[32m+[m[32m        return 0.0;[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m[32m    let mut sorted: Vec<f64> = samples.to_vec();[m
[32m+[m[32m    sorted.sort_by(|a, b| a.partial_cmp(b).unwrap_or(std::cmp::Ordering::Equal));[m
[32m+[m[32m    let idx = ((sorted.len() as f64 - 1.0) * 0.95).round() as usize;[m
[32m+[m[32m    sorted[idx.min(sorted.len() - 1)][m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m// ---------- integration tests (run via `cargo test`) ----------[m
[32m+[m

[32m+[m[32mcommand = "true"[m

[32m+[m[32mruns = 3[m

[32m+[m[32margs = [][m
[32m+[m[32mdescription = "integration test"[m
[32m+[m[32m"#[m
[32m+[m[32m        )[m
[32m+[m[32m        .unwrap();[m
[32m+[m[32m        let path = f.path().to_path_buf();[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m        let cfg = GateConfig {[m

[32m+[m[32m            fail_on_soft_regression: false,[m
[32m+[m[32m            output_format: OutputFormat::Text,[m
[32m+[m[32m        };[m
[32m+[m[32m        let gate = Gate::new(cfg).expect("gate loads");[m
[32m+[m[32m        assert_eq!(gate.budgets.len(), 1);[m
[32m+[m[32m        assert_eq!(gate.budgets[0].name, "pheno-config.parse_cargo");[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m        let verdict = evaluate_one(&gate.budgets[0]);[m
[32m+[m[32m        assert!(verdict.passed, "expected pass, got {:?}", verdict);[m
[32m+[m[32m        assert!(verdict.regressions.is_empty());[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    #[test][m
[32m+[m[32m    fn integration_test_fails_on_impossibly_low_budget() {[m
[32m+[m[32m        // p95_budget_ms = 0 forces a fail.[m
[32m+[m[32m        let mut f = tempfile::NamedTempFile::new().expect("tmpfile");[m
[32m+[m[32m        writeln!([m
[32m+[m[32m            f,[m
[32m+[m[32m            r#"[m
[32m+[m[32m[defaults][m
[32m+[m[32mruns = 2[m
[32m+[m[32mcommand = "true"[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m[pheno-x.too_tight][m
[32m+[m[32mp95_budget_ms = 0[m
[32m+[m[32mruns = 2[m
[32m+[m[32mcommand = "true"[m
[32m+[m[32margs = [][m
[32m+[m[32mdescription = "should always fail"[m
[32m+[m[32m"#[m
[32m+[m[32m        )[m
[32m+[m[32m        .unwrap();[m
[32m+[m[32m        let path = f.path().to_path_buf();[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m        let cfg = GateConfig {[m
[32m+[m[32m            perf_budgets_path: path,[m
[32m+[m[32m            fail_on_soft_regression: false,[m
[32m+[m[32m            output_format: OutputFormat::Json,[m
[32m+[m[32m        };[m
[32m+[m[32m        let gate = Gate::new(cfg).expect("gate loads");[m
[32m+[m[32m        let verdict = evaluate_one(&gate.budgets[0]);[m
[32m+[m[32m        assert!(!verdict.passed);[m
[32m+[m[32m        assert_eq!(verdict.regressions.len(), 1);[m
[32m+[m[32m        assert_eq!(verdict.regressions[0].level, RegressionLevel::Hard);[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m

[1m--- /dev/null[m

[36m@@ -0,0 +1,169 @@[m
[32m+[m[32m//! Budget type + classification — fleet-perf.toml → in-memory representation.[m
[32m+[m[32m//![m
[32m+[m[32m//! Authority: ADR-040 + v19 71-pillar cycle 9 plan §2 Track T4.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32muse serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};[m
[32m+[m[32muse std::collections::BTreeMap;[m
[32m+[m[32muse std::path::Path;[m
[32m+[m[32muse thiserror::Error;[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m/// Classification of a single measurement against its budget.[m
[32m+[m[32m#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)][m
[32m+[m[32mpub enum BudgetKind {[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Hard budget: a violation fails the gate (exit 1).[m
[32m+[m[32m    Hard,[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Soft budget: a violation is reported but does not fail the gate[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// (exit 2 only when `fail_on_soft_regression` is set).[m
[32m+[m[32m    Soft,[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m/// One declared budget, parsed from `fleet-perf.toml`.[m
[32m+[m[32m#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Serialize, Deserialize)][m
[32m+[m[32mpub struct PerformanceBudget {[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Fully-qualified name, e.g. `pheno-config.parse_cargo`.[m
[32m+[m[32m    pub name: String,[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// p95 ceiling in milliseconds.[m
[32m+[m[32m    pub p95_budget_ms: u64,[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Sample count for p95 computation.[m
[32m+[m[32m    pub runs: u32,[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Hard or soft.[m
[32m+[m[32m    pub kind: BudgetKind,[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Binary to invoke; defaults to `true` (no-op).[m
[32m+[m[32m    pub command: String,[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Args passed to the command.[m
[32m+[m[32m    pub args: Vec<String>,[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Human-readable summary.[m
[32m+[m[32m    pub description: String,[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m/// Outcome of evaluating one sample set against one budget.[m
[32m+[m[32m#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize)][m
[32m+[m[32mpub enum BudgetClassification {[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// p95 observed ≤ budget.[m
[32m+[m[32m    Pass,[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// p95 observed > budget; carries the overrun ratio for the regression record.[m
[32m+[m[32m    Fail,[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m/// Errors raised while parsing `fleet-perf.toml`.[m
[32m+[m[32m#[derive(Debug, Error)][m
[32m+[m[32mpub enum BudgetError {[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// File not found or unreadable.[m
[32m+[m[32m    #[error("I/O error reading budget file: {0}")][m
[32m+[m[32m    Io(#[from] std::io::Error),[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// TOML parse error.[m
[32m+[m[32m    #[error("TOML parse error: {0}")][m
[32m+[m[32m    Toml(#[from] toml::de::Error),[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m/// Raw shape of `benchmarks/fleet-perf.toml` (matches the v19 T4 schema).[m
[32m+[m[32m#[derive(Debug, Deserialize)][m
[32m+[m[32mpub(crate) struct RawManifest {[m
[32m+[m[32m    #[serde(default)][m
[32m+[m[32m    pub(crate) defaults: RawDefaults,[m
[32m+[m[32m    #[serde(flatten)][m
[32m+[m[32m    pub(crate) groups: BTreeMap<String, toml::Value>,[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m/// `[defaults]` section.[m
[32m+[m[32m#[derive(Debug, Deserialize, Default)][m
[32m+[m[32mpub(crate) struct RawDefaults {[m
[32m+[m[32m    pub(crate) runs: Option<u32>,[m
[32m+[m[32m    pub(crate) command: Option<String>,[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mimpl PerformanceBudget {[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Classify an observed p95 against this budget's ceiling.[m
[32m+[m[32m    pub fn classify(&self, p95_observed_ms: f64) -> BudgetClassification {[m
[32m+[m[32m        if p95_observed_ms <= self.p95_budget_ms as f64 {[m
[32m+[m[32m            BudgetClassification::Pass[m
[32m+[m[32m        } else {[m
[32m+[m[32m            BudgetClassification::Fail[m
[32m+[m[32m        }[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m/// Parse `fleet-perf.toml` into a flat list of `PerformanceBudget`.[m
[32m+[m[32m///[m
[32m+[m[32m/// The TOML shape is nested by crate (`[pheno-config.parse_cargo]`) and the[m
[32m+[m[32m/// "soft" classification is currently uniform (all budgets are Hard; this is[m
[32m+[m[32m/// the v19 T4 starting position and the `[meta].schema_doc` field cross-[m
[32m+[m[32m/// references ADR-026 + the 71-pillar schema for future extension).[m
[32m+[m[32mpub fn load_budgets_from_path(path: &Path) -> Result<Vec<PerformanceBudget>, BudgetError> {[m
[32m+[m[32m    let raw = std::fs::read_to_string(path)?;[m
[32m+[m[32m    let manifest: RawManifest = toml::from_str(&raw)?;[m
[32m+[m[32m    let default_runs = manifest.defaults.runs.unwrap_or(10);[m
[32m+[m[32m    let default_command = manifest.defaults.command.unwrap_or_else(|| "true".to_string());[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    let mut out = Vec::new();[m
[32m+[m[32m    for (group, value) in &manifest.groups {[m
[32m+[m[32m        if group == "meta" || group == "defaults" {[m
[32m+[m[32m            continue;[m
[32m+[m[32m        }[m
[32m+[m[32m        // Each group may be either a flat budget table OR a nested table of[m
[32m+[m[32m        // {method → budget}. Match both shapes; mirror perf_gate.py.[m
[32m+[m[32m        if value.get("p95_budget_ms").is_some() {[m
[32m+[m[32m            if let Some(budget) = parse_one(group.clone(), value, default_runs, &default_command) {[m
[32m+[m[32m                out.push(budget);[m
[32m+[m[32m            }[m
[32m+[m[32m        } else if let Some(table) = value.as_table() {[m
[32m+[m[32m            for (method, spec) in table {[m
[32m+[m[32m                if let Some(budget) = parse_one([m
[32m+[m[32m                    format!("{group}.{method}"),[m
[32m+[m[32m                    spec,[m
[32m+[m[32m                    default_runs,[m
[32m+[m[32m                    &default_command,[m
[32m+[m[32m                ) {[m
[32m+[m[32m                    out.push(budget);[m
[32m+[m[32m                }[m
[32m+[m[32m            }[m
[32m+[m[32m        }[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m[32m    Ok(out)[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mfn parse_one([m
[32m+[m[32m    name: String,[m
[32m+[m[32m    spec: &toml::Value,[m
[32m+[m[32m    default_runs: u32,[m
[32m+[m[32m    default_command: &str,[m
[32m+[m[32m) -> Option<PerformanceBudget> {[m
[32m+[m[32m    let table = spec.as_table()?;[m
[32m+[m[32m    let p95_budget_ms = table.get("p95_budget_ms")?.as_integer()? as u64;[m
[32m+[m[32m    let runs = table[m
[32m+[m[32m        .get("runs")[m
[32m+[m[32m        .and_then(|v| v.as_integer())[m
[32m+[m[32m        .map(|v| v as u32)[m
[32m+[m[32m        .unwrap_or(default_runs);[m
[32m+[m[32m    let command = table[m
[32m+[m[32m        .get("command")[m
[32m+[m[32m        .and_then(|v| v.as_str())[m
[32m+[m[32m        .unwrap_or(default_command)[m
[32m+[m[32m        .to_string();[m
[32m+[m[32m    let args = table[m
[32m+[m[32m        .get("args")[m
[32m+[m[32m        .and_then(|v| v.as_array())[m
[32m+[m[32m        .map(|arr| {[m
[32m+[m[32m            arr.iter()[m
[32m+[m[32m                .filter_map(|x| x.as_str().map(|s| s.to_string()))[m
[32m+[m[32m                .collect()[m
[32m+[m[32m        })[m
[32m+[m[32m        .unwrap_or_default();[m
[32m+[m[32m    let description = table[m
[32m+[m[32m        .get("description")[m
[32m+[m[32m        .and_then(|v| v.as_str())[m
[32m+[m[32m        .unwrap_or("")[m
[32m+[m[32m        .to_string();[m
[32m+[m[32m    // v19 T4 starting position: every declared budget is Hard. Soft budgets[m
[32m+[m[32m    // are a future extension — gated on the schema bump in benchmarks/fleet-perf.toml.[m
[32m+[m[32m    let kind = BudgetKind::Hard;[m
[32m+[m[32m    Some(PerformanceBudget {[m
[32m+[m[32m        name,[m
[32m+[m[32m        p95_budget_ms,[m
[32m+[m[32m        runs,[m
[32m+[m[32m        kind,[m
[32m+[m[32m        command,[m
[32m+[m[32m        args,[m
[32m+[m[32m        description,[m
[32m+[m[32m    })[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m

[1mnew file mode 100644[m
[1mindex 0000000000..15a6250cfb[m
[1m--- /dev/null[m
[1m+++ b/scripts/perf-gate/src/config.rs[m
[36m@@ -0,0 +1,129 @@[m
[32m+[m[32m//! Gate configuration — env + CLI overrides for the perf gate runner.[m
[32m+[m[32m//![m
[32m+[m[32m//! Authority: ADR-040 + v19 71-pillar cycle 9 plan §2 Track T4.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32muse std::path::PathBuf;[m
[32m+[m[32muse thiserror::Error;[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m/// Output format requested by the caller (or default `Text`).[m
[32m+[m[32m#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Default)][m
[32m+[m[32mpub enum OutputFormat {[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Plain-text human report.[m
[32m+[m[32m    #[default][m
[32m+[m[32m    Text,[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Machine-readable JSON.[m
[32m+[m[32m    Json,[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Markdown table.[m
[32m+[m[32m    Markdown,[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m/// Resolved configuration for a single `perf_gate` invocation.[m
[32m+[m[32m#[derive(Debug, Clone)][m
[32m+[m[32mpub struct GateConfig {[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Path to the `fleet-perf.toml` manifest.[m
[32m+[m[32m    pub perf_budgets_path: PathBuf,[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// When true, soft-budget regressions fail the gate (exit 2). When false,[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// soft regressions are reported only (exit 0 if no hard regressions).[m
[32m+[m[32m    pub fail_on_soft_regression: bool,[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// How to format the verdict in stdout.[m
[32m+[m[32m    pub output_format: OutputFormat,[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m/// Errors raised while building `GateConfig`.[m
[32m+[m[32m#[derive(Debug, Error)][m
[32m+[m[32mpub enum ConfigError {[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// `PERF_GATE_BUDGETS` pointed at a path that does not exist.[m
[32m+[m[32m    #[error("budget manifest not found at {0}")][m
[32m+[m[32m    MissingBudgets(PathBuf),[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Caller requested an unknown `--format` value.[m
[32m+[m[32m    #[error("invalid output format: {0}")][m
[32m+[m[32m    InvalidFormat(String),[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// I/O error while resolving the path.[m
[32m+[m[32m    #[error("I/O error resolving config: {0}")][m
[32m+[m[32m    Io(#[from] std::io::Error),[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mimpl GateConfig {[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Build a config from process environment variables.[m
[32m+[m[32m    ///[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Honors:[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// - `PERF_GATE_BUDGETS` — defaults to `benchmarks/fleet-perf.toml`.[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// - `PERF_GATE_FAIL_ON_SOFT` — `1` / `true` enables soft-regression failure.[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// - `PERF_GATE_FORMAT` — `text` / `json` / `markdown` (case-insensitive).[m
[32m+[m[32m    ///[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// This function does NOT validate that the budgets path exists; that[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// check happens in `Gate::new` via `load_budgets_from_path`. Callers that[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// want to surface a `MissingBudgets` error early should call[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// [`GateConfig::validate`] explicitly.[m
[32m+[m[32m    pub fn from_env() -> Result<Self, ConfigError> {[m
[32m+[m[32m        let pathbuf = PathBuf::from([m
[32m+[m[32m            std::env::var("PERF_GATE_BUDGETS")[m
[32m+[m[32m                .unwrap_or_else(|_| "benchmarks/fleet-perf.toml".to_string()),[m
[32m+[m[32m        );[m
[32m+[m[32m        let fail_on_soft_regression = matches!([m
[32m+[m[32m            std::env::var("PERF_GATE_FAIL_ON_SOFT").as_deref(),[m
[32m+[m[32m            Ok("1") | Ok("true") | Ok("TRUE") | Ok("yes")[m
[32m+[m[32m        );[m
[32m+[m[32m        let output_format = match std::env::var("PERF_GATE_FORMAT")[m
[32m+[m[32m            .as_deref()[m
[32m+[m[32m            .unwrap_or("text")[m
[32m+[m[32m            .to_ascii_lowercase()[m
[32m+[m[32m            .as_str()[m
[32m+[m[32m        {[m
[32m+[m[32m            "text" => OutputFormat::Text,[m
[32m+[m[32m            "json" => OutputFormat::Json,[m
[32m+[m[32m            "markdown" | "md" => OutputFormat::Markdown,[m
[32m+[m[32m            other => return Err(ConfigError::InvalidFormat(other.to_string())),[m
[32m+[m[32m        };[m
[32m+[m[32m        Ok(GateConfig {[m
[32m+[m[32m            perf_budgets_path: pathbuf,[m
[32m+[m[32m            fail_on_soft_regression,[m
[32m+[m[32m            output_format,[m
[32m+[m[32m        })[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Validate that the configured budgets path exists on disk.[m
[32m+[m[32m    pub fn validate(&self) -> Result<(), ConfigError> {[m
[32m+[m[32m        if !self.perf_budgets_path.exists() {[m
[32m+[m[32m            return Err(ConfigError::MissingBudgets(self.perf_budgets_path.clone()));[m
[32m+[m[32m        }[m
[32m+[m[32m        Ok(())[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m#[cfg(test)][m
[32m+[m[32mmod tests {[m
[32m+[m[32m    use super::*;[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    #[test][m
[32m+[m[32m    fn test_default_config_succeeds() {[m
[32m+[m[32m        // from_env must build a valid config when PERF_GATE_BUDGETS points at[m
[32m+[m[32m        // a path that exists. from_env itself does not validate path existence[m
[32m+[m[32m        // (see GateConfig::validate for that); the test asserts the path is[m
[32m+[m[32m        // set to the env value.[m
[32m+[m[32m        let mut f = tempfile::NamedTempFile::new().expect("tmpfile");[m
[32m+[m[32m        std::io::Write::write_all(&mut f, b"[meta]\nversion = \"t\"\n").expect("write");[m
[32m+[m[32m        let path = f.path().to_path_buf();[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m        let prev = std::env::var("PERF_GATE_BUDGETS").ok();[m
[32m+[m[32m        std::env::set_var("PERF_GATE_BUDGETS", &path);[m
[32m+[m[32m        let cfg = GateConfig::from_env().expect("from_env must build config without validating");[m
[32m+[m[32m        assert_eq!(cfg.perf_budgets_path, path);[m
[32m+[m[32m        assert_eq!(cfg.output_format, OutputFormat::Text);[m
[32m+[m[32m        // validate() must succeed for an existing path.[m
[32m+[m[32m        cfg.validate().expect("validate must succeed for existing path");[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m        // Default (unset) resolution.[m
[32m+[m[32m        std::env::remove_var("PERF_GATE_BUDGETS");[m
[32m+[m[32m        let cfg_default = GateConfig::from_env().expect("default resolution");[m
[32m+[m[32m        assert_eq!([m
[32m+[m[32m            cfg_default.perf_budgets_path,[m
[32m+[m[32m            PathBuf::from("benchmarks/fleet-perf.toml")[m
[32m+[m[32m        );[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m        if let Some(v) = prev {[m
[32m+[m[32m            std::env::set_var("PERF_GATE_BUDGETS", v);[m
[32m+[m[32m        }[m
[32m+[m[32m        // `f` is dropped at end of test → temp file deleted.[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m

[32m+[m[32m//! Gate — loads budgets and evaluates sample sets against them.[m
[32m+[m[32m//![m
[32m+[m[32m//! Authority: ADR-040 + v19 71-pillar cycle 9 plan §2 Track T4.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32muse crate::budgets::{load_budgets_from_path, BudgetError, PerformanceBudget};[m
[32m+[m[32muse crate::config::GateConfig;[m
[32m+[m[32muse thiserror::Error;[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m/// Severity of a single regression.[m
[32m+[m[32m#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq)][m
[32m+[m[32mpub enum RegressionLevel {[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Hard budget violated — exit 1.[m
[32m+[m[32m    Hard,[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Soft budget violated — exit 2 only if `fail_on_soft_regression`.[m
[32m+[m[32m    Soft,[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m/// One recorded regression.[m
[32m+[m[32m#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)][m
[32m+[m[32mpub struct Regression {[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Budget name (e.g. `pheno-config.parse_cargo`).[m
[32m+[m[32m    pub budget_name: String,[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Observed p95 in ms.[m
[32m+[m[32m    pub actual_ms: f64,[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Budgeted p95 ceiling in ms.[m
[32m+[m[32m    pub budget_ms: f64,[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Hard or soft.[m
[32m+[m[32m    pub level: RegressionLevel,[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m/// The verdict of evaluating a sample set against the loaded budgets.[m
[32m+[m[32m#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)][m
[32m+[m[32mpub struct GateVerdict {[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// True iff no Hard regression AND (no Soft regression OR `fail_on_soft_regression` is false).[m
[32m+[m[32m    pub passed: bool,[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// All regressions (Hard + Soft), empty on pass.[m
[32m+[m[32m    pub regressions: Vec<Regression>,[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Human-readable summary line.[m
[32m+[m[32m    pub summary: String,[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m/// Errors raised by the gate.[m
[32m+[m[32m#[derive(Debug, Error)][m
[32m+[m[32mpub enum GateError {[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Budget manifest could not be loaded.[m
[32m+[m[32m    #[error("failed to load budgets: {0}")][m
[32m+[m[32m    Budgets(#[from] BudgetError),[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m/// The gate — bundles config + parsed budgets + evaluation logic.[m
[32m+[m[32mpub struct Gate {[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Resolved configuration.[m
[32m+[m[32m    #[allow(dead_code)][m
[32m+[m[32m    pub config: GateConfig,[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Parsed budgets from the manifest.[m
[32m+[m[32m    pub budgets: Vec<PerformanceBudget>,[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mimpl Gate {[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Build a gate by reading the manifest at `config.perf_budgets_path`.[m
[32m+[m[32m    pub fn new(config: GateConfig) -> Result<Self, GateError> {[m
[32m+[m[32m        let budgets = load_budgets_from_path(&config.perf_budgets_path)?;[m
[32m+[m[32m        Ok(Self { config, budgets })[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Evaluate `samples` (interpreted as p95/p99 sample list in milliseconds)[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// against the *first* loaded budget. Returns a verdict describing the[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// pass/fail outcome and any regressions.[m
[32m+[m[32m    ///[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// When multiple budgets are loaded, callers should iterate and aggregate[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// via `summary::fleet_summary`.[m
[32m+[m[32m    pub fn evaluate(&self, samples: &[f64]) -> GateVerdict {[m
[32m+[m[32m        let mut regressions = Vec::new();[m
[32m+[m[32m        let p95 = p95_of(samples);[m
[32m+[m[32m        for budget in &self.budgets {[m
[32m+[m[32m            if matches!([m
[32m+[m[32m                budget.classify(p95),[m
[32m+[m[32m                crate::budgets::BudgetClassification::Fail[m
[32m+[m[32m            ) {[m
[32m+[m[32m                let level = match budget.kind {[m
[32m+[m[32m                    crate::budgets::BudgetKind::Hard => RegressionLevel::Hard,[m
[32m+[m[32m                    crate::budgets::BudgetKind::Soft => RegressionLevel::Soft,[m
[32m+[m[32m                };[m
[32m+[m[32m                regressions.push(Regression {[m
[32m+[m[32m                    budget_name: budget.name.clone(),[m
[32m+[m[32m                    actual_ms: p95,[m
[32m+[m[32m                    budget_ms: budget.p95_budget_ms as f64,[m
[32m+[m[32m                    level,[m
[32m+[m[32m                });[m
[32m+[m[32m            }[m
[32m+[m[32m        }[m
[32m+[m[32m        let hard_fail = regressions[m
[32m+[m[32m            .iter()[m
[32m+[m[32m            .any(|r| matches!(r.level, RegressionLevel::Hard));[m
[32m+[m[32m        let soft_fail = regressions[m
[32m+[m[32m            .iter()[m
[32m+[m[32m            .any(|r| matches!(r.level, RegressionLevel::Soft));[m
[32m+[m[32m        let passed = !hard_fail && (!soft_fail || !self.config.fail_on_soft_regression);[m
[32m+[m[32m        let summary = if regressions.is_empty() {[m
[32m+[m[32m            format!("all {} budgets within budget", self.budgets.len())[m
[32m+[m[32m        } else {[m
[32m+[m[32m            format!([m
[32m+[m[32m                "{} regressions across {} budgets",[m
[32m+[m[32m                regressions.len(),[m
[32m+[m[32m                self.budgets.len()[m
[32m+[m[32m            )[m
[32m+[m[32m        };[m
[32m+[m[32m        GateVerdict {[m
[32m+[m[32m            passed,[m
[32m+[m[32m            regressions,[m
[32m+[m[32m            summary,[m
[32m+[m[32m        }[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m/// Compute the p95 of a sample set. For empty input returns 0.0.[m
[32m+[m[32mfn p95_of(samples: &[f64]) -> f64 {[m
[32m+[m[32m    if samples.is_empty() {[m
[32m+[m[32m        return 0.0;[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m[32m    let mut sorted: Vec<f64> = samples.to_vec();[m
[32m+[m[32m    sorted.sort_by(|a, b| a.partial_cmp(b).unwrap_or(std::cmp::Ordering::Equal));[m
[32m+[m[32m    let idx = ((sorted.len() as f64 - 1.0) * 0.95).round() as usize;[m
[32m+[m[32m    sorted[idx.min(sorted.len() - 1)][m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m#[cfg(test)][m
[32m+[m[32mmod tests {[m
[32m+[m[32m    use super::*;[m
[32m+[m[32m    use crate::budgets::BudgetKind;[m
[32m+[m[32m    use crate::config::OutputFormat;[m
[32m+[m[32m    use std::io::Write;[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    fn cfg_with(path: std::path::PathBuf) -> GateConfig {[m
[32m+[m[32m        GateConfig {[m
[32m+[m[32m            perf_budgets_path: path,[m
[32m+[m[32m            fail_on_soft_regression: false,[m
[32m+[m[32m            output_format: OutputFormat::Text,[m
[32m+[m[32m        }[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    fn write_tmp_manifest(body: &str) -> (tempfile::NamedTempFile, std::path::PathBuf) {[m
[32m+[m[32m        let mut f = tempfile::NamedTempFile::new().expect("tmpfile");[m
[32m+[m[32m        f.write_all(body.as_bytes()).expect("write");[m
[32m+[m[32m        let path = f.path().to_path_buf();[m
[32m+[m[32m        (f, path)[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    const MANIFEST_ONE_BUDGET: &str = r#"[m
[32m+[m[32m[meta][m
[32m+[m[32mversion = "test"[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m[defaults][m
[32m+[m[32mruns = 10[m
[32m+[m[32mcommand = "true"[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m[pheno-config.parse_cargo][m
[32m+[m[32mp95_budget_ms = 50[m
[32m+[m[32mruns = 5[m
[32m+[m[32mcommand = "true"[m
[32m+[m[32margs = ["parse_cargo"][m
[32m+[m[32mdescription = "test"[m
[32m+[m[32m"#;[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    #[test][m
[32m+[m[32m    fn test_evaluate_pass_within_budget() {[m
[32m+[m[32m        let (_f, path) = write_tmp_manifest(MANIFEST_ONE_BUDGET);[m
[32m+[m[32m        let gate = Gate::new(cfg_with(path)).expect("gate loads");[m
[32m+[m[32m        // p95 of [1..10] ms is ≤ budget 50.[m
[32m+[m[32m        let verdict = gate.evaluate(&(1..=10).map(|x| x as f64).collect::<Vec<_>>());[m
[32m+[m[32m        assert!(verdict.passed, "expected pass, got {:?}", verdict);[m
[32m+[m[32m        assert!(verdict.regressions.is_empty());[m
[32m+[m[32m        assert!(verdict.summary.contains("within budget"));[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    #[test][m
[32m+[m[32m    fn test_evaluate_fail_over_budget() {[m
[32m+[m[32m        let (_f, path) = write_tmp_manifest(MANIFEST_ONE_BUDGET);[m
[32m+[m[32m        let gate = Gate::new(cfg_with(path)).expect("gate loads");[m
[32m+[m[32m        // All samples 100 ms → p95 = 100 > budget 50.[m
[32m+[m[32m        let verdict = gate.evaluate(&vec![100.0; 10]);[m
[32m+[m[32m        assert!(!verdict.passed, "expected fail, got {:?}", verdict);[m
[32m+[m[32m        assert_eq!(verdict.regressions.len(), 1);[m
[32m+[m[32m        assert_eq!([m
[32m+[m[32m            verdict.regressions[0].budget_name,[m
[32m+[m[32m            "pheno-config.parse_cargo"[m
[32m+[m[32m        );[m
[32m+[m[32m        assert_eq!(verdict.regressions[0].level, RegressionLevel::Hard);[m
[32m+[m[32m        assert!((verdict.regressions[0].budget_ms - 50.0).abs() < 1e-9);[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    #[test][m
[32m+[m[32m    fn test_soft_regression_does_not_fail_when_not_required() {[m
[32m+[m[32m        // Soft budget violation should NOT fail when fail_on_soft_regression is false.[m
[32m+[m[32m        let (_f, path) = write_tmp_manifest([m
[32m+[m[32m            r#"[m
[32m+[m[32m[defaults][m
[32m+[m[32mruns = 5[m
[32m+[m[32mcommand = "true"[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m[pheno-x.soft_method][m
[32m+[m[32mp95_budget_ms = 1[m
[32m+[m[32mruns = 5[m
[32m+[m[32mcommand = "true"[m
[32m+[m[32m"#,[m
[32m+[m[32m        );[m
[32m+[m[32m        let cfg = GateConfig {[m
[32m+[m[32m            perf_budgets_path: path,[m
[32m+[m[32m            fail_on_soft_regression: false,[m
[32m+[m[32m            output_format: OutputFormat::Text,[m
[32m+[m[32m        };[m
[32m+[m[32m        // Override the loaded budget to be Soft.[m
[32m+[m[32m        let mut gate = Gate::new(cfg).expect("gate loads");[m
[32m+[m[32m        gate.budgets[0].kind = BudgetKind::Soft;[m
[32m+[m[32m        let verdict = gate.evaluate(&vec![10.0; 5]);[m
[32m+[m[32m        assert!(verdict.passed, "soft-only should pass when not required");[m
[32m+[m[32m        assert_eq!(verdict.regressions.len(), 1);[m
[32m+[m[32m        assert_eq!(verdict.regressions[0].level, RegressionLevel::Soft);[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m

[32m+[m[32m//! scripts/perf-gate — fleet performance gate (v19 T4, L19 Performance Benchmarks).[m
[32m+[m[32m//![m
[32m+[m[32m//! Loads `benchmarks/fleet-perf.toml`, evaluates measured p95 samples against[m
[32m+[m[32m//! each method's declared budget, and renders a verdict (Pass / Fail).[m
[32m+[m[32m//![m
[32m+[m[32m//! Authority: ADR-040 (test coverage gates per tier) + v19 71-pillar cycle 9[m
[32m+[m[32m//! plan §2 Track T4. See `plans/2026-06-21-v19-71-pillar-cycle-9-p0.md`.[m
[32m+[m[32m//![m
[32m+[m[32m//! The binary `perf_gate` lives in `src/bin/perf_gate.rs`. The Python[m
[32m+[m[32m//! implementation in `scripts/perf_gate.py` is kept as a legacy alternative.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m#![forbid(unsafe_code)][m
[32m+[m[32m#![warn(missing_docs)][m

[32m+[m[32mpub mod summary;[m
