[32m+[m[32m//! Reporter — format a `GateVerdict` for human or machine readers.[m
[32m+[m[32m//![m
[32m+[m[32m//! Authority: ADR-040 + v19 71-pillar cycle 9 plan §2 Track T4.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32muse crate::gate::{GateVerdict, RegressionLevel};[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m/// A reporter renders a `GateVerdict` to a string.[m
[32m+[m[32mpub trait Reporter {[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// Render the verdict. Implementations must be deterministic so the[m
[32m+[m[32m    /// nightly + PR runs produce stable diffs in `findings/`.[m
[32m+[m[32m    fn render(&self, verdict: &GateVerdict) -> String;[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m/// Plain-text reporter — default for human reading in CI logs.[m
[32m+[m[32mpub struct TextReporter;[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mimpl Reporter for TextReporter {[m
[32m+[m[32m    fn render(&self, verdict: &GateVerdict) -> String {[m
[32m+[m[32m        let mut out = String::new();[m
[32m+[m[32m        out.push_str(if verdict.passed {[m
[32m+[m[32m            "PASS: "[m
[32m+[m[32m        } else {[m
[32m+[m[32m            "FAIL: "[m
[32m+[m[32m        });[m
[32m+[m[32m        out.push_str(&verdict.summary);[m
[32m+[m[32m        out.push('\n');[m
[32m+[m[32m        if !verdict.regressions.is_empty() {[m
[32m+[m[32m            out.push_str("regressions:\n");[m
[32m+[m[32m            for r in &verdict.regressions {[m
[32m+[m[32m                let level = match r.level {[m
[32m+[m[32m                    RegressionLevel::Hard => "HARD",[m
[32m+[m[32m                    RegressionLevel::Soft => "SOFT",[m
[32m+[m[32m                };[m
[32m+[m[32m                out.push_str(&format!([m
[32m+[m[32m                    "  - [{level}] {name}: {actual:.3} ms > {budget:.3} ms\n",[m
[32m+[m[32m                    level = level,[m
[32m+[m[32m                    name = r.budget_name,[m
[32m+[m[32m                    actual = r.actual_ms,[m
[32m+[m[32m                    budget = r.budget_ms,[m
[32m+[m[32m                ));[m
[32m+[m[32m            }[m
[32m+[m[32m        }[m
[32m+[m[32m        out[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m/// JSON reporter — for downstream tools and artifact upload.[m
[32m+[m[32mpub struct JsonReporter;[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mimpl Reporter for JsonReporter {[m
[32m+[m[32m    fn render(&self, verdict: &GateVerdict) -> String {[m
[32m+[m[32m        // Hand-rolled JSON to avoid pulling in a JSON crate; the verdict shape[m
[32m+[m[32m        // is small and stable.[m
[32m+[m[32m        let mut s = String::from("{\n");[m
[32m+[m[32m        s.push_str(&format!("  \"passed\": {},\n", verdict.passed));[m
[32m+[m[32m        s.push_str(&format!([m
[32m+[m[32m            "  \"summary\": {},\n",[m
[32m+[m[32m            json_string(&verdict.summary)[m
[32m+[m[32m        ));[m
[32m+[m[32m        s.push_str("  \"regressions\": [");[m
[32m+[m[32m        if verdict.regressions.is_empty() {[m
[32m+[m[32m            s.push(']');[m
[32m+[m[32m        } else {[m
[32m+[m[32m            s.push('\n');[m
[32m+[m[32m            for (i, r) in verdict.regressions.iter().enumerate() {[m
[32m+[m[32m                let comma = if i + 1 < verdict.regressions.len() { "," } else { "" };[m
[32m+[m[32m                let level = match r.level {[m
[32m+[m[32m                    RegressionLevel::Hard => "hard",[m
[32m+[m[32m                    RegressionLevel::Soft => "soft",[m
[32m+[m[32m                };[m
[32m+[m[32m                s.push_str(&format!([m
[32m+[m[32m                    "    {{\"budget\": {}, \"actual_ms\": {:.3}, \"budget_ms\": {:.3}, \"level\": \"{}\"}}{}\n",[m
[32m+[m[32m                    json_string(&r.budget_name),[m
[32m+[m[32m                    r.actual_ms,[m
[32m+[m[32m                    r.budget_ms,[m
[32m+[m[32m                    level,[m
[32m+[m[32m                    comma[m
[32m+[m[32m                ));[m
[32m+[m[32m            }[m
[32m+[m[32m            s.push_str("  ]");[m
[32m+[m[32m        }[m
[32m+[m[32m        s.push_str("\n}\n");[m
[32m+[m[32m        s[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m/// Markdown reporter — for the GitHub Actions PR comment and findings/.[m
[32m+[m[32mpub struct MarkdownReporter;[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mimpl Reporter for MarkdownReporter {[m
[32m+[m[32m    fn render(&self, verdict: &GateVerdict) -> String {[m
[32m+[m[32m        let mut out = String::new();[m
[32m+[m[32m        out.push_str("## Perf gate verdict\n\n");[m
[32m+[m[32m        let icon = if verdict.passed { "✅" } else { "❌" };[m
[32m+[m[32m        out.push_str(&format!([m
[32m+[m[32m            "{} **{}** — {}\n\n",[m
[32m+[m[32m            icon,[m
[32m+[m[32m            if verdict.passed { "PASS" } else { "FAIL" },[m
[32m+[m[32m            verdict.summary[m
[32m+[m[32m        ));[m
[32m+[m[32m        if !verdict.regressions.is_empty() {[m
[32m+[m[32m            out.push_str("| budget | actual (ms) | budget (ms) | level |\n");[m
[32m+[m[32m            out.push_str("|---|---:|---:|---|\n");[m
[32m+[m[32m            for r in &verdict.regressions {[m
[32m+[m[32m                let level = match r.level {[m
[32m+[m[32m                    RegressionLevel::Hard => "HARD",[m
[32m+[m[32m                    RegressionLevel::Soft => "SOFT",[m
[32m+[m[32m                };[m
[32m+[m[32m                out.push_str(&format!([m
[32m+[m[32m                    "| {} | {:.3} | {:.3} | {} |\n",[m
[32m+[m[32m                    r.budget_name, r.actual_ms, r.budget_ms, level[m
[32m+[m[32m                ));[m
[32m+[m[32m            }[m
[32m+[m[32m        }[m
[32m+[m[32m        out.push('\n');[m
[32m+[m[32m        out[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mfn json_string(s: &str) -> String {[m
[32m+[m[32m    let mut out = String::from("\"");[m
[32m+[m[32m    for c in s.chars() {[m
[32m+[m[32m        match c {[m
[32m+[m[32m            '"' => out.push_str("\\\""),[m
[32m+[m[32m            '\\' => out.push_str("\\\\"),[m
[32m+[m[32m            '\n' => out.push_str("\\n"),[m
[32m+[m[32m            '\r' => out.push_str("\\r"),[m
[32m+[m[32m            '\t' => out.push_str("\\t"),[m
[32m+[m[32m            c if (c as u32) < 0x20 => out.push_str(&format!("\\u{:04x}", c as u32)),[m
[32m+[m[32m            c => out.push(c),[m
[32m+[m[32m        }[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m[32m    out.push('"');[m
[32m+[m[32m    out[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m

[32m+[m[32m//! Fleet-level summary aggregation across multiple `GateVerdict`s.[m
[32m+[m[32m//![m
[32m+[m[32m//! Authority: ADR-040 + v19 71-pillar cycle 9 plan §2 Track T4.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32muse crate::gate::{GateVerdict, RegressionLevel};[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m/// Aggregate multiple verdicts into a single human-readable summary line.[m
[32m+[m[32m///[m
[32m+[m[32m/// Output shape (stable across nightly + PR runs so PR-comment diffs are[m
[32m+[m[32m/// readable):[m
[32m+[m[32m///[m
[32m+[m[32m/// ```text[m
[32m+[m[32m/// {n} budgets: {passed} passed, {failed} failed[m
[32m+[m[32m/// ```[m
[32m+[m[32m///[m
[32m+[m[32m/// If exactly one verdict failed, the summary appends a parenthetical naming[m
[32m+[m[32m/// the first failing budget so reviewers can scan PR comments quickly.[m
[32m+[m[32mpub fn fleet_summary(verdicts: &[GateVerdict]) -> String {[m
[32m+[m[32m    let total = verdicts.len();[m
[32m+[m[32m    let passed = verdicts.iter().filter(|v| v.passed).count();[m
[32m+[m[32m    let failed = total - passed;[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    let mut out = format!("{total} budgets: {passed} passed, {failed} failed");[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    if failed == 1 {[m
[32m+[m[32m        if let Some(v) = verdicts.iter().find(|v| !v.passed) {[m
[32m+[m[32m            if let Some(r) = v[m
[32m+[m[32m                .regressions[m
[32m+[m[32m                .iter()[m
[32m+[m[32m                .find(|r| matches!(r.level, RegressionLevel::Hard))[m
[32m+[m[32m                .or_else(|| v.regressions.first())[m
[32m+[m[32m            {[m
[32m+[m[32m                out.push_str(&format!(" (L19 regression in {})", r.budget_name));[m
[32m+[m[32m            }[m
[32m+[m[32m        }[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m[32m    out[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m#[cfg(test)][m
[32m+[m[32mmod tests {[m
[32m+[m[32m    use super::*;[m
[32m+[m[32m    use crate::gate::Regression;[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    fn v(passed: bool, name: &str) -> GateVerdict {[m
[32m+[m[32m        GateVerdict {[m
[32m+[m[32m            passed,[m
[32m+[m[32m            summary: "s".into(),[m
[32m+[m[32m            regressions: if passed {[m
[32m+[m[32m                Vec::new()[m
[32m+[m[32m            } else {[m
[32m+[m[32m                vec![Regression {[m
[32m+[m[32m                    budget_name: name.into(),[m
[32m+[m[32m                    actual_ms: 100.0,[m
[32m+[m[32m                    budget_ms: 50.0,[m
[32m+[m[32m                    level: RegressionLevel::Hard,[m
[32m+[m[32m                }][m
[32m+[m[32m            },[m
[32m+[m[32m        }[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    #[test][m
[32m+[m[32m    fn test_fleet_summary_aggregates_correctly() {[m
[32m+[m[32m        let verdicts = vec![v(true, "x"), v(true, "y"), v(false, "pheno-config.parse_cargo")];[m
[32m+[m[32m        let s = fleet_summary(&verdicts);[m
[32m+[m[32m        assert_eq!(s, "3 budgets: 2 passed, 1 failed (L19 regression in pheno-config.parse_cargo)");[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    #[test][m
[32m+[m[32m    fn test_fleet_summary_all_pass() {[m
[32m+[m[32m        let verdicts = vec![v(true, "x"), v(true, "y")];[m
[32m+[m[32m        let s = fleet_summary(&verdicts);[m
[32m+[m[32m        assert_eq!(s, "2 budgets: 2 passed, 0 failed");[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    #[test][m
[32m+[m[32m    fn test_fleet_summary_empty() {[m
[32m+[m[32m        let s = fleet_summary(&[]);[m
[32m+[m[32m        assert_eq!(s, "0 budgets: 0 passed, 0 failed");[m
[32m+[m[32m    }[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m

[32m+[m[32m#!/usr/bin/env python3[m
[32m+[m[32m"""scripts/perf_gate.py — v19 T4 perf gate runner.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mLoads benchmarks/fleet-perf.toml, runs each benchmark N times, computes p95,[m
[32m+[m[32masserts against budget. Exit 0 if all pass, 1 otherwise. Writes a Markdown[m
[32m+[m[32mreport + JSON results to findings/perf-<date>.{txt,json}.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mAuthority: ADR-040 + v19 71-pillar cycle 9 P0 plan §2 Track T4.[m
[32m+[m[32m"""[m
[32m+[m[32mimport argparse, json, statistics, subprocess, sys, time[m
[32m+[m[32mfrom datetime import datetime, timezone[m
[32m+[m[32mfrom pathlib import Path[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mtry:[m
[32m+[m[32m    import tomllib[m
[32m+[m[32mexcept ImportError:[m
[32m+[m[32m    import tomli as tomllib[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mdef load_manifest(p: Path) -> dict:[m
[32m+[m[32m    with p.open("rb") as f:[m
[32m+[m[32m        return tomllib.load(f)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mdef time_cmd(cmd, runs):[m
[32m+[m[32m    out = [][m
[32m+[m[32m    for _ in range(runs):[m
[32m+[m[32m        t0 = time.perf_counter()[m
[32m+[m[32m        subprocess.run(cmd, check=False, capture_output=True)[m
[32m+[m[32m        out.append((time.perf_counter() - t0) * 1000.0)[m
[32m+[m[32m    return out[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mdef p95(s):[m
[32m+[m[32m    s = sorted(s)[m
[32m+[m[32m    return s[max(0, int(round(0.95 * (len(s) - 1))))][m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mdef run_one(name, spec, defaults):[m
[32m+[m[32m    runs = spec.get("runs", defaults.get("runs", 10))[m
[32m+[m[32m    budget = spec["p95_budget_ms"][m
[32m+[m[32m    cmd = [spec.get("command", defaults.get("command", "true"))] + list(spec.get("args", []))[m
[32m+[m[32m    samples = time_cmd(cmd, runs)[m
[32m+[m[32m    obs = p95(samples)[m
[32m+[m[32m    return {"name": name, "command": cmd, "runs": runs,[m
[32m+[m[32m            "p95_ms": round(obs, 3), "budget_ms": budget,[m
[32m+[m[32m            "passed": obs <= budget, "samples_ms": [round(x, 3) for x in samples]}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mdef render(results, started):[m
[32m+[m[32m    L = [f"# Perf gate report — {started}\n",[m
[32m+[m[32m         "| benchmark | p95 (ms) | budget (ms) | runs | status |",[m
[32m+[m[32m         "|-----------|---------:|------------:|-----:|--------|"][m
[32m+[m[32m    for r in results:[m
[32m+[m[32m        L.append(f"| {r['name']} | {r['p95_ms']} | {r['budget_ms']} | {r['runs']} | {'PASS' if r['passed'] else 'FAIL'} |")[m
[32m+[m[32m    fail = sum(1 for r in results if not r["passed"])[m
[32m+[m[32m    L += ["", f"Total: {len(results)}, Failed: {fail}", ""][m
[32m+[m[32m    return "\n".join(L)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mdef main():[m
[32m+[m[32m    ap = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="v19 T4 perf gate runner")[m
[32m+[m[32m    ap.add_argument("--manifest", required=True, type=Path)[m
[32m+[m[32m    ap.add_argument("--findings-dir", type=Path, default=Path("findings"))[m
[32m+[m[32m    args = ap.parse_args()[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    manifest = load_manifest(args.manifest)[m
[32m+[m[32m    defaults = manifest.get("defaults", {})[m
[32m+[m[32m    started = datetime.now(timezone.utc).strftime("%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ")[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    results = [][m
[32m+[m[32m    for group, entries in manifest.items():[m
[32m+[m[32m        if group in {"meta", "defaults"}:[m
[32m+[m[32m            continue[m
[32m+[m[32m        # Flat form: "name" -> {p95_budget_ms: ...}; group form: "crate" -> {"method": {...}}[m
[32m+[m[32m        if not isinstance(entries, dict) or "p95_budget_ms" in entries:[m
[32m+[m[32m            entries = {group: entries}[m
[32m+[m[32m        for name, spec in entries.items():[m
[32m+[m[32m            if not isinstance(spec, dict) or "p95_budget_ms" not in spec:[m
[32m+[m[32m                continue[m
[32m+[m[32m            results.append(run_one(f"{group}.{name}", spec, defaults))[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    report = render(results, started)[m
[32m+[m[32m    print(report)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    args.findings_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)[m
[32m+[m[32m    stamp = datetime.now(timezone.utc).strftime("%Y-%m-%d")[m
[32m+[m[32m    (args.findings_dir / f"perf-{stamp}.txt").write_text(report + "\n")[m
[32m+[m[32m    (args.findings_dir / f"perf-{stamp}.json").write_text(json.dumps(results, indent=2) + "\n")[m
[32m+[m[32m    print(f"Wrote: findings/perf-{stamp}.{{txt,json}}", file=sys.stderr)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m    return 0 if all(r["passed"] for r in results) else 1[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mif __name__ == "__main__":[m
[32m+[m[32m    sys.exit(main())[m

[32m+[m[32m#!/bin/bash[m
[32m+[m[32mset -euo pipefail[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mREPO_DIR="$1"[m
[32m+[m[32mcd "$REPO_DIR" || { echo "ERROR: Cannot cd to $REPO_DIR"; exit 1; }[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mREPO_NAME=$(basename "$(pwd)")[m
[32m+[m[32mERRORS=""[m
[32m+[m[32mPUSHED=""[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# Step 2: fetch[m
[32m+[m[32mgit fetch origin 2>&1 || ERRORS+="FETCH_FAILED;"[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# Step 3: current branch[m
[32m+[m[32mBRANCH=$(git symbolic-ref --short HEAD 2>/dev/null || echo "DETACHED")[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# Step 4: stashes[m
[32m+[m[32mSTASHES=$(git stash list 2>/dev/null | wc -l || echo 0)[m
[32m+[m[32mSTASHES=$((STASHES + 0))[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# Step 5: dirty files[m
[32m+[m[32mDIRTY=$(git status --porcelain 2>/dev/null | wc -l || echo 0)[m
[32m+[m[32mDIRTY=$((DIRTY + 0))[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mecho "REPO=$REPO_NAME BRANCH=$BRANCH STASHES=$STASHES DIRTY=$DIRTY"[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# Step 6: local-only branches[m
[32m+[m[32mLOCAL_ONLY=""[m
[32m+[m[32mfor b in $(git branch --format='%(refname:short)' 2>/dev/null); do[m
[32m+[m[32m  if ! git show-ref --verify --quiet "refs/remotes/origin/$b" 2>/dev/null; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    LOCAL_ONLY="$LOCAL_ONLY $b"[m
[32m+[m[32m    echo "LOCAL_ONLY:$b"[m
[32m+[m[32m  fi[m
[32m+[m[32mdone[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# Step 7: unpushed commits[m
[32m+[m[32mecho "UNPUSHED_COMMITS:"[m
[32m+[m[32mgit log --oneline @{u}..HEAD 2>/dev/null | head -5 || echo "(no upstream or no unpushed)"[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m### TAKE ACTION ###[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# === DETACHED HEAD ===[m
[32m+[m[32mif [ "$BRANCH" = "DETACHED" ]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m  echo "DETACHED_HEAD: creating branch"[m
[32m+[m[32m  git checkout -b "wip/detached-2026-06-17" 2>&1 || true[m
[32m+[m[32m  if git push origin "wip/detached-2026-06-17" 2>&1; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    PUSHED="$PUSHED wip/detached-2026-06-17"[m
[32m+[m[32m  else[m
[32m+[m[32m    ERRORS+="PUSH_FAILED:wip/detached-2026-06-17;"[m
[32m+[m[32m  fi[m
[32m+[m[32m  BRANCH="wip/detached-2026-06-17"[m
[32m+[m[32mfi[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# === DIRTY WORKTREE ===[m
[32m+[m[32mif [ "$DIRTY" -gt 0 ]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m  echo "DIRTY_WORKTREE: committing dirty state"[m
[32m+[m[32m  git add -A 2>&1 || true[m
[32m+[m[32m  if git commit -m "wip: save dirty state [auto]" 2>&1; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    echo "COMMIT_OK"[m
[32m+[m[32m  else[m
[32m+[m[32m    echo "COMMIT_FAILED: trying stash"[m
[32m+[m[32m    git stash 2>&1 || true[m
[32m+[m[32m    NEW_STASHES=$(git stash list 2>/dev/null | wc -l || echo 0)[m
[32m+[m[32m    STASHES=$((NEW_STASHES + 0))[m
[32m+[m[32m  fi[m
[32m+[m[32mfi[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# === STASHES ===[m
[32m+[m[32mif [ "$STASHES" -gt 0 ]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m  echo "STASHES_FOUND: processing..."[m
[32m+[m[32m  git stash list --format="%gd|%s" 2>/dev/null | while IFS='|' read -r stash_ref stash_msg; do[m
[32m+[m[32m    SLUG=$(echo "$stash_msg" | sed 's/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/ /g' | tr -s ' ' | xargs | tr ' ' '-' | tr '[:upper:]' '[:lower:]' | cut -c1-80)[m
[32m+[m[32m    BRANCH_NAME="wip/${SLUG}-2026-06-17"[m
[32m+[m[32m    echo "Stash: $stash_ref -> $BRANCH_NAME"[m
[32m+[m[32m    if git stash branch "$BRANCH_NAME" "$stash_ref" 2>/dev/null; then[m
[32m+[m[32m      if git push origin "$BRANCH_NAME" 2>&1; then[m
[32m+[m[32m        echo "PUSHED:$BRANCH_NAME"[m
[32m+[m[32m      else[m
[32m+[m[32m        echo "PUSH_FAILED:$BRANCH_NAME"[m
[32m+[m[32m      fi[m
[32m+[m[32m      git checkout "$BRANCH" 2>/dev/null || echo "CHECKOUT_FAILED:$BRANCH"[m
[32m+[m[32m    else[m
[32m+[m[32m      echo "STASH_BRANCH_FAILED:$stash_ref"[m
[32m+[m[32m    fi[m
[32m+[m[32m  done[m
[32m+[m[32mfi[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# === LOCAL-ONLY BRANCHES ===[m
[32m+[m[32mfor branch in $LOCAL_ONLY; do[m
[32m+[m[32m  echo "PUSHING_LOCAL_ONLY:$branch"[m
[32m+[m[32m  if git push origin "$branch" 2>&1; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    PUSHED="$PUSHED $branch"[m
[32m+[m[32m  else[m
[32m+[m[32m    ERRORS+="PUSH_FAILED:$branch;"[m
[32m+[m[32m  fi[m
[32m+[m[32mdone[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# === UNPUSHED COMMITS - push current branch ===[m
[32m+[m[32mecho "PUSHING_CURRENT_BRANCH:$BRANCH"[m
[32m+[m[32mif git push origin "$BRANCH" 2>&1; then[m
[32m+[m[32m  PUSHED="$PUSHED $BRANCH"[m
[32m+[m[32m  STATUS="ok"[m
[32m+[m[32melse[m
[32m+[m[32m  ERRORS+="PUSH_FAILED:$BRANCH;"[m
[32m+[m[32m  STATUS="error"[m
[32m+[m[32mfi[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mPUSHED_CLEAN=$(echo "$PUSHED" | xargs | tr ' ' ',')[m
[32m+[m[32mecho ""[m
[32m+[m[32mecho "REPO=$REPO_NAME STATUS=$STATUS STASHES=$STASHES DIRTY=$DIRTY PUSHED=$PUSHED_CLEAN"[m
[32m+[m[32mif [ -n "$ERRORS" ]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m  echo "ERRORS=$ERRORS"[m
[32m+[m[32mfi[m

[32m+[m[32m#!/usr/bin/env bash[m
[32m+[m[32m# scripts/ssot_inject.sh — v14 Class A stub for the ssot-inject CI gate.[m
[32m+[m[32m#[m
[32m+[m[32m# Auto-injects any required SSOT.md sections that are missing. The full[m
[32m+[m[32m# implementation is staged for a follow-up cycle; this stub is the contract[m
[32m+[m[32m# surface the .github/workflows/ssot-inject.yml workflow expects.[m
[32m+[m[32m#[m
[32m+[m[32m# Per ADR-022 (config consolidation — two-crate canonical split), the[m
[32m+[m[32m# authoritative SSOT validator is scripts/validate-ssot.sh. This script[m
[32m+[m[32m# is a forward-compatible injection shim that exits 0 in both modes.[m
[32m+[m[32m#[m
[32m+[m[32m# Usage:[m
[32m+[m[32m#   scripts/ssot_inject.sh           # perform injection (currently noop)[m
[32m+[m[32m#   scripts/ssot_inject.sh --dry-run # report missing sections, do not modify[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mset -euo pipefail[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# Always run from the repo root so relative paths in the workflow match.[m
[32m+[m[32mREPO_ROOT="$(git rev-parse --show-toplevel 2>/dev/null || pwd)"[m
[32m+[m[32mcd "$REPO_ROOT"[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mDRY_RUN=0[m
[32m+[m[32mif [[ "${1:-}" == "--dry-run" ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    DRY_RUN=1[m
[32m+[m[32mfi[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# Sections required by ADR-022 / SSOT contract.[m
[32m+[m[32mREQUIRED_SECTIONS=([m
[32m+[m[32m    "Scope"[m
[32m+[m[32m    "Precedence order"[m
[32m+[m[32m    "Updating this file"[m
[32m+[m[32m)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mmissing=()[m
[32m+[m[32mif [[ -f SSOT.md ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    for section in "${REQUIRED_SECTIONS[@]}"; do[m
[32m+[m[32m        if ! grep -qE "^## .*${section}" SSOT.md; then[m
[32m+[m[32m            missing+=("$section")[m
[32m+[m[32m        fi[m
[32m+[m[32m    done[m
[32m+[m[32melse[m
[32m+[m[32m    missing+=("(SSOT.md missing)")[m
[32m+[m[32mfi[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mif [[ ${#missing[@]} -gt 0 ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    echo "[ssot-inject] missing sections: ${missing[*]}"[m
[32m+[m[32mfi[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mif [[ "$DRY_RUN" -eq 1 ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    echo "[ssot-inject] dry-run: no changes"[m
[32m+[m[32m    exit 0[m
[32m+[m[32mfi[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# Real injection logic is staged for the next 71-pillar cycle. For now this[m
[32m+[m[32m# is a noop that delegates to the canonical validator.[m
[32m+[m[32mif [[ -x ./scripts/validate-ssot.sh ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    ./scripts/validate-ssot.sh[m
[32m+[m[32melse[m
[32m+[m[32m    echo "[ssot-inject] noop — see scripts/validate-ssot.sh"[m
[32m+[m[32mfi[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mexit 0[m
[1mdiff --git a/scripts/test-all.sh b/scripts/test-all.sh[m
[1mnew file mode 100755[m
[1mindex 0000000000..e50e55ca94[m
[1m--- /dev/null[m
[1m+++ b/scripts/test-all.sh[m
[36m@@ -0,0 +1,377 @@[m
[32m+[m[32m#!/usr/bin/env bash[m
[32m+[m[32m# scripts/test-all.sh — SIDE-20 workspace-level test runner.[m
[32m+[m[32m#[m
[32m+[m[32m# Iterates every pheno-* crate visible on this checkout, detects its[m
[32m+[m[32m# primary language by manifest file, and runs the appropriate test[m
[32m+[m[32m# command (cargo test for Rust, pytest for Python, npm test for[m
[32m+[m[32m# TypeScript). Aggregates pass/fail/ignored counts per crate and[m
[32m+[m[32m# writes a structured JSON report to test-results/<UTC-date>.json.[m
[32m+[m[32m#[m
[32m+[m[32m# Usage:[m
[32m+[m[32m#   scripts/test-all.sh                      # run all pheno-* crates[m
[32m+[m[32m#   scripts/test-all.sh pheno-config pheno-errors   # run a subset[m
[32m+[m[32m#   scripts/test-all.sh --rust-only          # skip python/ts/unknown[m
[32m+[m[32m#   scripts/test-all.sh --no-fail-fast       # keep going on failures[m
[32m+[m[32m#[m
[32m+[m[32m# Authority: SIDE-20 (2026-06-22). See findings/2026-06-22-SIDE-20-test-runner.md.[m
[32m+[m[32m#[m
[32m+[m[32m# Exit code: 0 if every detected crate's tests passed; 1 otherwise.[m
[32m+[m[32m# Always writes the JSON report before exiting so partial runs still[m
[32m+[m[32m# produce a result file.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mset -uo pipefail[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# ── Defaults ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────[m
[32m+[m[32mSCRIPT_NAME="test-all"[m
[32m+[m[32mSCHEMA_VERSION="1"[m
[32m+[m[32mWORKSPACE_ROOT="$(git rev-parse --show-toplevel 2>/dev/null || pwd)"[m
[32m+[m[32mTEST_RESULTS_DIR="${WORKSPACE_ROOT}/test-results"[m
[32m+[m[32mRUST_ONLY=0[m
[32m+[m[32mPYTHON_ONLY=0[m
[32m+[m[32mNO_FAIL_FAST=0[m
[32m+[m[32mSELECTED_CRATES=()[m
[32m+[m[32mUTC_DATE="$(date -u +%Y-%m-%d)"[m
[32m+[m[32mUTC_TIMESTAMP="$(date -u +%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ)"[m
[32m+[m[32mRESULT_FILE="${TEST_RESULTS_DIR}/${UTC_DATE}.json"[m
[32m+[m[32mLOGS_DIR="${TEST_RESULTS_DIR}/logs/${UTC_DATE}"[m
[32m+[m[32m# Per-crate wall-clock budget in seconds. 0 = no timeout.[m
[32m+[m[32m# Override via TIMEOUT_PER_CRATE_SECS env var (CI: 1800, dev: 120).[m
[32m+[m[32mTIMEOUT_PER_CRATE_SECS="${TIMEOUT_PER_CRATE_SECS:-300}"[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# ── Args ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────[m
[32m+[m[32mfor arg in "$@"; do[m
[32m+[m[32m  case "$arg" in[m
[32m+[m[32m    --rust-only)         RUST_ONLY=1 ;;[m
[32m+[m[32m    --python-only)       PYTHON_ONLY=1 ;;[m
[32m+[m[32m    --no-fail-fast)      NO_FAIL_FAST=1 ;;[m
[32m+[m[32m    --timeout=*)         TIMEOUT_PER_CRATE_SECS="${arg#--timeout=}" ;;[m
[32m+[m[32m    -h|--help)[m
[32m+[m[32m      sed -n '2,16p' "$0"[m
[32m+[m[32m      exit 0[m
[32m+[m[32m      ;;[m
[32m+[m[32m    --*)                 echo "unknown flag: $arg" >&2; exit 2 ;;[m
[32m+[m[32m    *)                   SELECTED_CRATES+=("$arg") ;;[m
[32m+[m[32m  esac[m
[32m+[m[32mdone[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mmkdir -p "$TEST_RESULTS_DIR" "$LOGS_DIR"[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# ── Helpers ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────[m
[32m+[m[32mlog() { printf '[%s] %s\n' "$(date -u +%H:%M:%S)" "$*"; }[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# Detect a crate's primary language by manifest file. Emits one of:[m
[32m+[m[32m#   rust | python | ts | unknown[m
[32m+[m[32mdetect_language() {[m
[32m+[m[32m  local d="$1"[m
[32m+[m[32m  if [[ -f "$d/Cargo.toml" ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    echo "rust"[m
[32m+[m[32m  elif [[ -f "$d/pyproject.toml" || -f "$d/setup.py" ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    echo "python"[m
[32m+[m[32m  elif [[ -f "$d/package.json" ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    echo "ts"[m
[32m+[m[32m  else[m
[32m+[m[32m    echo "unknown"[m
[32m+[m[32m  fi[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# Resolve the test command for a crate/language pair. Echoes a[m
[32m+[m[32m# space-separated string: "<command> | <args...>" — split by callers[m
[32m+[m[32m# via a sentinel pipe separator.[m
[32m+[m[32mtest_command_for() {[m
[32m+[m[32m  local lang="$1" crate="$2"[m
[32m+[m[32m  case "$lang" in[m
[32m+[m[32m    rust)[m
[32m+[m[32m      # Each pheno-* Rust crate is standalone (no parent workspace at[m
[32m+[m[32m      # the monorepo root), so `cd` into the crate and run plain[m
[32m+[m[32m      # `cargo test`. This is equivalent to `cargo test -p <crate>`[m
[32m+[m[32m      # from a workspace root.[m
[32m+[m[32m      echo "cargo test --no-fail-fast --color=never"[m
[32m+[m[32m      ;;[m
[32m+[m[32m    python)[m
[32m+[m[32m      if [[ -f "$crate/pyproject.toml" ]] && grep -q '\[tool.pytest' "$crate/pyproject.toml" 2>/dev/null; then[m
[32m+[m[32m        echo "python -m pytest --tb=short -q"[m
[32m+[m[32m      elif command -v pytest >/dev/null 2>&1; then[m
[32m+[m[32m        echo "pytest --tb=short -q"[m
[32m+[m[32m      else[m
[32m+[m[32m        echo "python -m unittest discover -s tests -t . -v"[m
[32m+[m[32m      fi[m
[32m+[m[32m      ;;[m
[32m+[m[32m    ts)[m
[32m+[m[32m      echo "npm test --silent"[m
[32m+[m[32m      ;;[m
[32m+[m[32m    *)[m
[32m+[m[32m      echo ""[m
[32m+[m[32m      ;;[m
[32m+[m[32m  esac[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# Parse "test result: ok. N passed; M failed; K ignored; ..." from cargo[m
[32m+[m[32m# output. Echoes "passed|failed|ignored" with -1 for unknown.[m
[32m+[m[32mparse_cargo_counts() {[m
[32m+[m[32m  local logfile="$1"[m
[32m+[m[32m  # The summary line looks like: "test result: ok. 42 passed; 0 failed; 0 ignored; ..."[m
[32m+[m[32m  # or "test result: FAILED. 5 passed; 3 failed; 0 ignored; ..."[m
[32m+[m[32m  # Pull the LAST occurrence (cargo prints one per test binary).[m
[32m+[m[32m  local line[m
[32m+[m[32m  line=$(grep -E '^test result:' "$logfile" 2>/dev/null | tail -n 1 || true)[m
[32m+[m[32m  if [[ -z "$line" ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    echo "-1|-1|-1"[m
[32m+[m[32m    return[m
[32m+[m[32m  fi[m
[32m+[m[32m  local p f i[m
[32m+[m[32m  p=$(echo "$line" | sed -nE 's/.* ([0-9]+) passed.*/\1/p')[m
[32m+[m[32m  f=$(echo "$line" | sed -nE 's/.* ([0-9]+) failed.*/\1/p')[m
[32m+[m[32m  i=$(echo "$line" | sed -nE 's/.* ([0-9]+) ignored.*/\1/p')[m
[32m+[m[32m  [[ -z "$p" ]] && p=0[m
[32m+[m[32m  [[ -z "$f" ]] && f=0[m
[32m+[m[32m  [[ -z "$i" ]] && i=0[m
[32m+[m[32m  echo "${p}|${f}|${i}"[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# Parse "= N passed, M failed, K error in T.TTs =" from pytest.[m
[32m+[m[32mparse_pytest_counts() {[m
[32m+[m[32m  local logfile="$1"[m
[32m+[m[32m  local line[m
[32m+[m[32m  line=$(grep -E '^=.*passed.*(failed|error).*in ' "$logfile" 2>/dev/null | tail -n 1 || true)[m
[32m+[m[32m  if [[ -z "$line" ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    # All-pass form: "= N passed in T.TTs ="[m
[32m+[m[32m    line=$(grep -E '^= .* passed in ' "$logfile" 2>/dev/null | tail -n 1 || true)[m
[32m+[m[32m    if [[ -n "$line" ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m      local p[m
[32m+[m[32m      p=$(echo "$line" | sed -nE 's/^= ([0-9]+) passed.*/\1/p')[m
[32m+[m[32m      echo "${p:-0}|0|0"[m
[32m+[m[32m      return[m
[32m+[m[32m    fi[m
[32m+[m[32m    # All-skip form[m
[32m+[m[32m    line=$(grep -E '^= .* skipped in ' "$logfile" 2>/dev/null | tail -n 1 || true)[m
[32m+[m[32m    if [[ -n "$line" ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m      echo "0|0|-1"[m
[32m+[m[32m      return[m
[32m+[m[32m    fi[m
[32m+[m[32m    echo "-1|-1|-1"[m
[32m+[m[32m    return[m
[32m+[m[32m  fi[m
[32m+[m[32m  local p f e[m
[32m+[m[32m  p=$(echo "$line" | sed -nE 's/^= ([0-9]+) passed.*/\1/p')[m
[32m+[m[32m  f=$(echo "$line" | sed -nE 's/.* ([0-9]+) failed.*/\1/p')[m
[32m+[m[32m  e=$(echo "$line" | sed -nE 's/.* ([0-9]+) error.*/\1/p')[m
[32m+[m[32m  echo "${p:-0}|${f:-0}|${e:-0}"[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# json_escape — emit a string safely for inclusion inside a JSON value.[m
[32m+[m[32mjson_escape() {[m
[32m+[m[32m  local s="${1//\\/\\\\}"[m
[32m+[m[32m  s="${s//\"/\\\"}"[m
[32m+[m[32m  s="${s//	/\\t}"[m
[32m+[m[32m  printf '%s' "$s"[m
[32m+[m[32m}[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# ── Discover crates ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────[m
[32m+[m[32mif [[ ${#SELECTED_CRATES[@]} -gt 0 ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m  CRATES=("${SELECTED_CRATES[@]}")[m
[32m+[m[32melse[m
[32m+[m[32m  # `find` from repo root for top-level pheno-* directories only.[m
[32m+[m[32m  # Use a portable pattern that works on both GNU find (Linux CI) and[m
[32m+[m[32m  # BSD find (macOS dev). We strip the leading "./" prefix below.[m
[32m+[m[32m  while IFS= read -r d; do[m
[32m+[m[32m    d="${d#./}"[m
[32m+[m[32m    CRATES+=("$d")[m
[32m+[m[32m  done < <(cd "$WORKSPACE_ROOT" && find . -maxdepth 1 -mindepth 1 -type d -name 'pheno-*' | sort)[m
[32m+[m[32mfi[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mif [[ ${#CRATES[@]} -eq 0 ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m  log "no pheno-* crates found under ${WORKSPACE_ROOT}"[m
[32m+[m[32m  exit 1[m
[32m+[m[32mfi[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mlog "discovered ${#CRATES[@]} pheno-* crate(s) under ${WORKSPACE_ROOT}"[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# ── Run tests per crate ─────────────────────────────────────────────────[m
[32m+[m[32m# We build a JSON array of per-crate result objects in a tempfile, then[m
[32m+[m[32m# splice into the final report. This avoids quoting headaches.[m
[32m+[m[32mPER_CRATE_JSON="$(mktemp -t test-all.XXXXXX.json)"[m
[32m+[m[32mtrap 'rm -f "$PER_CRATE_JSON"' EXIT[m
[32m+[m[32m: > "$PER_CRATE_JSON"[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mTOTAL_PASSED=0[m
[32m+[m[32mTOTAL_FAILED=0[m
[32m+[m[32mTOTAL_IGNORED=0[m
[32m+[m[32mCRATES_PASSED=0[m
[32m+[m[32mCRATES_FAILED=0[m
[32m+[m[32mCRATES_SKIPPED=0[m
[32m+[m[32mFIRST_FAILURE=""[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mfor crate in "${CRATES[@]}"; do[m
[32m+[m[32m  crate_path="${WORKSPACE_ROOT}/${crate}"[m
[32m+[m[32m  if [[ ! -d "$crate_path" ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    log "WARN: ${crate} directory not found, skipping"[m
[32m+[m[32m    continue[m
[32m+[m[32m  fi[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m  lang="$(detect_language "$crate_path")"[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m  # Filter by language selection flags.[m
[32m+[m[32m  if [[ "$RUST_ONLY" == "1" && "$lang" != "rust" ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    continue[m
[32m+[m[32m  fi[m
[32m+[m[32m  if [[ "$PYTHON_ONLY" == "1" && "$lang" != "python" ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    continue[m
[32m+[m[32m  fi[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m  cmd="$(test_command_for "$lang" "$crate_path")"[m
[32m+[m[32m  log_file="${LOGS_DIR}/${crate}.log"[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m  if [[ "$lang" == "unknown" || -z "$cmd" ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    log "[$crate] lang=$lang  →  skipped (no test manifest)"[m
[32m+[m[32m    CRATES_SKIPPED=$((CRATES_SKIPPED + 1))[m
[32m+[m[32m    cat >> "$PER_CRATE_JSON" <<EOF[m
[32m+[m[32m{"crate":"$(json_escape "$crate")","language":"$lang","status":"skipped","reason":"no test manifest","passed":0,"failed":0,"ignored":0,"duration_ms":0,"exit_code":-1,"log_file":"$(json_escape "logs/${UTC_DATE}/${crate}.log")","command":""},[m
[32m+[m[32mEOF[m
[32m+[m[32m    continue[m
[32m+[m[32m  fi[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m  log "[$crate] lang=$lang  cmd='$cmd'"[m
[32m+[m[32m  start_ns=$(date +%s%N)[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m  # Run with an optional wall-clock timeout. `gtimeout` (macOS coreutils)[m
[32m+[m[32m  # falls back to `timeout` (Linux CI). A zero timeout means unbounded.[m
[32m+[m[32m  timed_out=0[m
[32m+[m[32m  if [[ "$TIMEOUT_PER_CRATE_SECS" -gt 0 ]] && command -v timeout >/dev/null 2>&1; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    # shellcheck disable=SC2086[m
[32m+[m[32m    ( cd "$crate_path" && timeout "${TIMEOUT_PER_CRATE_SECS}s" $cmd ) > "$log_file" 2>&1[m
[32m+[m[32m    rc=$?[m
[32m+[m[32m    # timeout(1) exits 124 on timeout; mark it explicitly.[m
[32m+[m[32m    if [[ "$rc" == "124" ]]; then timed_out=1; fi[m
[32m+[m[32m  else[m
[32m+[m[32m    # shellcheck disable=SC2086[m
[32m+[m[32m    ( cd "$crate_path" && $cmd ) > "$log_file" 2>&1[m
[32m+[m[32m    rc=$?[m
[32m+[m[32m  fi[m
[32m+[m[32m  end_ns=$(date +%s%N)[m
[32m+[m[32m  duration_ms=$(( (end_ns - start_ns) / 1000000 ))[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m  case "$lang" in[m
[32m+[m[32m    rust)   counts="$(parse_cargo_counts "$log_file")" ;;[m
[32m+[m[32m    python) counts="$(parse_pytest_counts "$log_file")" ;;[m
[32m+[m[32m    *)      counts="0|0|0" ;;[m
[32m+[m[32m  esac[m
[32m+[m[32m  p="${counts%%|*}"[m
[32m+[m[32m  rest="${counts#*|}"[m
[32m+[m[32m  f="${rest%%|*}"[m
[32m+[m[32m  i="${rest#*|}"[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m  # Timeout short-circuits all status logic below.[m
[32m+[m[32m  if [[ "$timed_out" == "1" ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    status="timeout"[m
[32m+[m[32m    p=-1; f=-1; i=-1[m
[32m+[m[32m    CRATES_FAILED=$((CRATES_FAILED + 1))[m
[32m+[m[32m    [[ -z "$FIRST_FAILURE" ]] && FIRST_FAILURE="$crate"[m
[32m+[m[32m  elif [[ "$p" == "-1" ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    # Parsing yielded no summary line — fall back to exit code.[m
[32m+[m[32m    if [[ "$rc" == "0" ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m      status="passed"[m
[32m+[m[32m      p=0; f=0; i=0[m
[32m+[m[32m      CRATES_PASSED=$((CRATES_PASSED + 1))[m
[32m+[m[32m    else[m
[32m+[m[32m      status="failed"[m
[32m+[m[32m      p=0; f=0; i=0[m
[32m+[m[32m      CRATES_FAILED=$((CRATES_FAILED + 1))[m
[32m+[m[32m      [[ -z "$FIRST_FAILURE" ]] && FIRST_FAILURE="$crate"[m
[32m+[m[32m    fi[m
[32m+[m[32m  elif [[ "$rc" == "0" && "$f" == "0" ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    status="passed"[m
[32m+[m[32m    CRATES_PASSED=$((CRATES_PASSED + 1))[m
[32m+[m[32m  else[m
[32m+[m[32m    status="failed"[m
[32m+[m[32m    CRATES_FAILED=$((CRATES_FAILED + 1))[m
[32m+[m[32m    [[ -z "$FIRST_FAILURE" ]] && FIRST_FAILURE="$crate"[m
[32m+[m[32m  fi[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m  # Skip the totals bookkeeping for timeout entries — their counts are[m
[32m+[m[32m  # sentinel -1 and would corrupt the aggregate sums.[m
[32m+[m[32m  if [[ "$timed_out" != "1" ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    TOTAL_PASSED=$((TOTAL_PASSED + p))[m
[32m+[m[32m    TOTAL_FAILED=$((TOTAL_FAILED + f))[m
[32m+[m[32m    TOTAL_IGNORED=$((TOTAL_IGNORED + i))[m
[32m+[m[32m  fi[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m  log "[$crate] status=$status  passed=$p failed=$f ignored=$i  rc=$rc  ${duration_ms}ms"[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m  cat >> "$PER_CRATE_JSON" <<EOF[m
[32m+[m[32m{"crate":"$(json_escape "$crate")","language":"$lang","status":"$status","passed":$p,"failed":$f,"ignored":$i,"duration_ms":$duration_ms,"exit_code":$rc,"log_file":"$(json_escape "logs/${UTC_DATE}/${crate}.log")","command":"$(json_escape "$cmd")"},[m
[32m+[m[32mEOF[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m  if [[ "$status" == "failed" && "$NO_FAIL_FAST" == "0" ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m    log "stopping on first failure (re-run with --no-fail-fast to continue)"[m
[32m+[m[32m    break[m
[32m+[m[32m  fi[m
[32m+[m[32mdone[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# Strip the trailing comma so we have a clean JSON array. Avoid[m
[32m+[m[32m# `sed -i` (BSD/GNU differ on macOS) — use Python, which is already[m
[32m+[m[32m# a workflow dep per test-all.yml.[m
[32m+[m[32mif [[ -s "$PER_CRATE_JSON" ]]; then[m
[32m+[m[32m  python3 - "$PER_CRATE_JSON" <<'PYEOF'[m
[32m+[m[32mimport sys[m
[32m+[m[32mp = sys.argv[1][m
[32m+[m[32mwith open(p) as f:[m
[32m+[m[32m    lines = f.readlines()[m
[32m+[m[32mif lines and lines[-1].rstrip().endswith(','):[m
[32m+[m[32m    lines[-1] = lines[-1].rstrip('\n').rstrip(',') + '\n'[m
[32m+[m[32mwith open(p, 'w') as f:[m
[32m+[m[32m    f.writelines(lines)[m
[32m+[m[32mPYEOF[m
[32m+[m[32mfi[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# ── Toolchain info ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────[m
[32m+[m[32mRUST_VERSION=""[m
[32m+[m[32mif command -v cargo >/dev/null 2>&1; then[m
[32m+[m[32m  RUST_VERSION="$(rustc --version 2>/dev/null || cargo --version)"[m
[32m+[m[32mfi[m
[32m+[m[32mPY_VERSION=""[m
[32m+[m[32mif command -v python3 >/dev/null 2>&1; then[m
[32m+[m[32m  PY_VERSION="$(python3 --version 2>&1)"[m
[32m+[m[32mfi[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# ── Emit final JSON report ──────────────────────────────────────────────[m
[32m+[m[32m{[m
[32m+[m[32m  printf '{\n'[m
[32m+[m[32m  printf '  "schema_version": "%s",\n'                "$SCHEMA_VERSION"[m
[32m+[m[32m  printf '  "script": "%s",\n'                        "$SCRIPT_NAME"[m
[32m+[m[32m  printf '  "timestamp_utc": "%s",\n'                 "$UTC_TIMESTAMP"[m
[32m+[m[32m  printf '  "workspace_root": "%s",\n'                "$(json_escape "$WORKSPACE_ROOT")"[m
[32m+[m[32m  printf '  "result_file": "%s",\n'                   "$(json_escape "${UTC_DATE}.json")"[m
[32m+[m[32m  printf '  "toolchain": {\n'[m
[32m+[m[32m  printf '    "rust": "%s",\n'                        "$(json_escape "$RUST_VERSION")"[m
[32m+[m[32m  printf '    "python": "%s"\n'                       "$(json_escape "$PY_VERSION")"[m
[32m+[m[32m  printf '  },\n'[m
[32m+[m[32m  printf '  "summary": {\n'[m
[32m+[m[32m  printf '    "crates_total": %d,\n'                  "${#CRATES[@]}"[m
[32m+[m[32m  printf '    "crates_passed": %d,\n'                 "$CRATES_PASSED"[m
[32m+[m[32m  printf '    "crates_failed": %d,\n'                 "$CRATES_FAILED"[m
[32m+[m[32m  printf '    "crates_skipped": %d,\n'                "$CRATES_SKIPPED"[m
[32m+[m[32m  printf '    "tests_passed": %d,\n'                  "$TOTAL_PASSED"[m
[32m+[m[32m  printf '    "tests_failed": %d,\n'                  "$TOTAL_FAILED"[m
[32m+[m[32m  printf '    "tests_ignored": %d,\n'                 "$TOTAL_IGNORED"[m
[32m+[m[32m  printf '    "first_failure": "%s"\n'                "$(json_escape "$FIRST_FAILURE")"[m
[32m+[m[32m  printf '  },\n'[m
[32m+[m[32m  printf '  "crates": [\n'[m
[32m+[m[32m  cat "$PER_CRATE_JSON"[m
[32m+[m[32m  printf '  ]\n'[m
[32m+[m[32m  printf '}\n'[m
[32m+[m[32m} > "$RESULT_FILE"[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mlog "wrote ${RESULT_FILE}"[m
[32m+[m

[32m+[m[32m#!/usr/bin/env bash[m
[32m+[m[32m# scripts/vault_smoke.sh — L50 Vault smoke test (ADR-077, ADR-079)[m
[32m+[m[32m#[m
[32m+[m[32m# Verifies a Vault dev server is reachable, accepts a write, returns the value[m
[32m+[m[32m# on read, and that dynamic credentials can be rotated (different value on[m
[32m+[m[32m# each request when the path is a dynamic engine like aws/creds/*).[m
[32m+[m[32m#[m
[32m+[m[32m# Usage:[m
[32m+[m[32m#   VAULT_ADDR=http://127.0.0.1:8200 VAULT_TOKEN=root ./scripts/vault_smoke.sh[m
[32m+[m[32m#[m
[32m+[m[32m# Defaults assume `vault server -dev` is running on localhost.[m
[32m+[m[32m#[m
[32m+[m[32m# Exit codes:[m
[32m+[m[32m#   0 — all checks passed.[m
[32m+[m[32m#   1 — Vault unreachable, unauthenticated, or a check failed.[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mset -euo pipefail[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mVAULT_ADDR="${VAULT_ADDR:-http://127.0.0.1:8200}"[m
[32m+[m[32mVAULT_TOKEN="${VAULT_TOKEN:-root}"[m
[32m+[m[32mTEST_PATH="secret/data/pheno/dev/smoke/test"[m
[32m+[m[32mTEST_KEY="rotating_value"[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# Pre-flight: jq + curl required[m
[32m+[m[32mfor bin in curl jq; do[m
[32m+[m[32m  command -v "$bin" >/dev/null 2>&1 || { echo "missing dep: $bin" >&2; exit 1; }[m
[32m+[m[32mdone[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# 1. Health check[m
[32m+[m[32mstatus=$(curl -sf "${VAULT_ADDR}/v1/sys/health" | jq -r '.initialized')[m
[32m+[m[32m[[ "$status" == "true" ]] || { echo "FAIL: vault not initialized at ${VAULT_ADDR}" >&2; exit 1; }[m
[32m+[m[32mecho "OK: vault initialized at ${VAULT_ADDR}"[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# 2. Write a test secret (PUT to KV v2 — payload wrapped in {"data":{...}})[m
[32m+[m[32mcurl -sf -X POST -H "X-Vault-Token: ${VAULT_TOKEN}" \[m
[32m+[m[32m  --data "{\"data\":{\"${TEST_KEY}\":\"v1-$(date +%s)\"}}" \[m
[32m+[m[32m  "${VAULT_ADDR}/v1/${TEST_PATH}" >/dev/null[m
[32m+[m[32mecho "OK: wrote test secret to ${TEST_PATH}"[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# 3. Read + decrypt the secret; assert the value is non-empty[m
[32m+[m[32mread_value=$(curl -sf -H "X-Vault-Token: ${VAULT_TOKEN}" \[m
[32m+[m[32m  "${VAULT_ADDR}/v1/${TEST_PATH}" | jq -r ".data.data.${TEST_KEY}")[m
[32m+[m[32m[[ -n "$read_value" && "$read_value" != "null" ]] || { echo "FAIL: read returned empty" >&2; exit 1; }[m
[32m+[m[32mecho "OK: read back value=${read_value}"[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# 4. Rotate: write a new value; verify subsequent read returns the new value[m
[32m+[m[32mnew_value="v2-$(date +%s)-rotated"[m
[32m+[m[32mcurl -sf -X POST -H "X-Vault-Token: ${VAULT_TOKEN}" \[m
[32m+[m[32m  --data "{\"data\":{\"${TEST_KEY}\":\"${new_value}\"}}" \[m
[32m+[m[32m  "${VAULT_ADDR}/v1/${TEST_PATH}" >/dev/null[m
[32m+[m[32mrotated_value=$(curl -sf -H "X-Vault-Token: ${VAULT_TOKEN}" \[m
[32m+[m[32m  "${VAULT_ADDR}/v1/${TEST_PATH}" | jq -r ".data.data.${TEST_KEY}")[m
[32m+[m[32m[[ "$rotated_value" == "$new_value" ]] || { echo "FAIL: rotation did not propagate (got=${rotated_value})" >&2; exit 1; }[m
[32m+[m[32mecho "OK: rotation propagated (got=${rotated_value})"[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32m# 5. Optional dynamic-engine probe (only if aws engine mounted)[m
[32m+[m[32mif curl -sf -H "X-Vault-Token: ${VAULT_TOKEN}" "${VAULT_ADDR}/v1/sys/mounts" | jq -e '.["aws/"]' >/dev/null 2>&1; then[m
[32m+[m[32m  d1=$(curl -sf -H "X-Vault-Token: ${VAULT_TOKEN}" "${VAULT_ADDR}/v1/aws/creds/smoke" | jq -r '.data.access_key')[m
[32m+[m[32m  d2=$(curl -sf -H "X-Vault-Token: ${VAULT_TOKEN}" "${VAULT_ADDR}/v1/aws/creds/smoke" | jq -r '.data.access_key')[m
[32m+[m[32m  [[ "$d1" != "$d2" && -n "$d1" && "$d1" != "null" ]] || { echo "FAIL: dynamic creds not rotating" >&2; exit 1; }[m
[32m+[m[32m  echo "OK: dynamic creds rotate (d1=${d1:0:8}... d2=${d2:0:8}...)"[m
[32m+[m[32mfi[m
[32m+[m
[32m+[m[32mecho "PASS: vault_smoke.sh — all checks green"[m
\ No newline at end of file[m
